Important News

Memorial Week for the Central Government and the National Government

Central Party Headquarters

At 9 a.m. on the 11th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 72nd Memorial Week for the Premier in the auditorium. Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Enke Batu, Miao Peicheng, etc., as well as staff from various departments and guests, numbered about 500 people. Chairman Chen Guofu bowed, and then the chairman's report briefly stated: "Regarding the military aspect, the Central Army has captured Tai'an and is surrounding Jinan. Although the Feng rebel troops on the Longhai Line have repeatedly tried their best to counterattack, they have all been defeated. In the recent period, the anti-rebellion military can definitely achieve a great victory and eliminate the rebel troops. There is a definite grasp. After the recapture of Changsha, the tragic suffering of the people was unprecedented. Personnel have now been sent to investigate the details in order to properly appease them. The reason why the Communist Party is so rampant this time is that most of the Central Army was sent to the front to suppress the rebellion. One part of He Jian's troops was stationed in southern Hunan and could not be transferred in time. The defenses of Changsha were inevitably empty, so it was suddenly captured. The most important reason is that the Yan-Feng warlords and reorganizationists saw that the military affairs of the central government were progressing step by step and their own destiny was in danger, so they tried their best to collude with the Communist Party to disrupt our army's rear and attempt to contain a part of the military force, thus causing the tragedy of Changsha. During this period, they still loudly proclaimed anti-communism and prominently unveiled the slogan of exterminating the Communist Party in order to cover up their heinous crimes, deceiving themselves and others, who would believe it. Now, the main forces of Yan and Feng have been defeated and disintegrated. In the present, as soon as the suppression of the rebellion is completed, moving troops to destroy the communists will definitely be like crushing dry weeds and destroying decaying matter. It is not difficult to eliminate them in one fell swoop. After Wang Jingwei arrived in Beiping, the so-called expanded meeting is being greatly publicized. Generally, people believe that it will have some impact on the central government. The reactionaries are especially elated, but the loyal comrades and people of our party who have common sense all regard it as a ridiculous move, no different from seeking their own destruction. In terms of the cause and effect of things, anyone who wants to be the leader of a party must be able to lead the comrades within the party and all the people to follow the doctrine and create happiness for the country and the people, use the credit earned to gain the belief of the people, and must be determined in his integrity and not be swayed by wealth or subdued by force. Only in this way can he bear the heavy expectations of a party and gain sympathy and support. If he flatters the warlords and seeks to achieve personal desires, and is willing to be used by the traitors, then his personality has long been lost. Can he still claim to be the leader? The newspaper reported the other day that Wang had a letter to Qi Xieyuan, actually calling him Comrade Fuwan. Even a three-foot-tall child knows that Qi is a reactionary warlord, but he actually cited him as a fellow traveler, which is not surprising. Also, looking at the newspaper report on his plan to organize a government, he first wants to establish a Supervisory Yuan and an Examination Yuan, and how to organize other high-level agencies is silent and absurd, bizarre and incomprehensible, making people feel at a loss. It is appropriate to see that his days are numbered, his mind is exhausted and his skills are exhausted. After the report was over, the meeting was adjourned.

National Government

At 10 a.m. on the same morning, the National Government held the Premier's Memorial Week. Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Ma Fuxiang, Yi Peiji, Jiang Menglin, Wang Boqun, Zhang Nanxian, Liu Ruiheng, Lin Xiang, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Zheng Hongnian, Mu Xiangchuan, Zhou Yawei, Wu Siyu, Qin Hua, Chen Yu, etc., and more than 200 officials from the civil and military affairs offices attended. After Chairman Tan Yankai bowed, Secretary Qian Changzhao gave the following political report: "The Jinpu Road in Jinan can be recovered within days. The rebels on the Longhai Road believe that our full force is concentrated on Jinpu and that the attempt to counterattack will cause great losses. Xuchang on the Pinghan Road is under siege and can be captured soon. Roughly, the military affairs can be concluded within a month. As for the area of Changsha, after the communist harassment, it will take some time to restore its vitality in the future. The government is very concerned about this and feels very distressed. The harm of the Communist Party has been going on for more than a day or two. Murders and arson have occurred from time to time in the provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. The government should have launched a large-scale encirclement and suppression to solve the problem once and for all. However, military rebellions have occurred repeatedly in recent years, and the government has had no choice but to use force. Although it has been gradually pacified, the communists everywhere have been able to survive. Now it is even more rampant than before and cannot be solved immediately. The State Council resolved last Friday that He Yingqin, the director of the Bandit Suppression Affairs of the E, Xiang and Gan Dynasties, was specially appointed to be responsible for handling the bandit suppression affairs. The garrisons of each province are all under the command of the director. At this moment, we think about the rebellion of feudal warlords, the harassment of the Communist Party, and the disturbances of local bandits, and all the final struggles of reactionary elements have created a phenomenon of unrest in the locality. The strength of the government can definitely eliminate them, but we must know that in addition to the general unrest in the country, there are really many social ills. For example, the general poverty, the general weakness, the general backwardness of knowledge, the general decline of righteousness, and the general lack of national consciousness are all equally serious. It is okay to talk about them separately. (1) The general poverty. Although there are no statistics on the property of the people in our country, we refer to local surveys in various aspects. The poor account for at least 70% of the people. The so-called poor, of course, refers to compatriots who cannot maintain or have difficulty maintaining the minimum living standard. Recently, the living standard has become higher and higher, especially after the trend of valuing gold and devaluing silver, it has become more difficult. Even those with a little property can only barely survive, and there are not many people who can be said to be rich in the whole country. At this time of hardship, foreign oppression continues to come, and domestic production cannot immediately make it develop. The danger of the economic future is really unbearable. (2) The general weakness. There is no denying the weakness of our Chinese race. Generally, people have poor health, are plagued by diseases, and plagues occur from time to time. There are not enough Western doctors to distribute in society, and traditional Chinese medicine does not understand science. Western medicines cannot be manufactured themselves and rely entirely on imports. Chinese medicines do not know how to organize, and public health and sports are not emphasized at all. No wonder the race is weakening day by day. According to the speculation of many scholars, the population of our country is only decreasing and not increasing. That is, the mortality rate of all the recent population statistics in various places mostly exceeds the productivity rate. We must know that in the world, the superior races will be defeated, and if we do not try to remedy the situation urgently, we will inevitably gradually disappear. (3) The general backwardness of knowledge. Everyone knows that education in our country is not universal. No matter where you are, there are always too few elementary schools, and it is even more difficult to find a complete elementary school. As for the middle schools and universities, they are not necessarily very good. Therefore, most parents are suspicious of sending their children to school, so the number of people who have the opportunity to go to school is reduced, and the knowledge of the majority of people is also backward. In this 20th century, if you want to live, if you have backward knowledge, even if you can avoid freezing and starving, you will inevitably be exploited. This is a natural result. (4) The general decline of righteousness. There are really too few people in society who can treat people and things with righteousness. The evil and corrupt atmosphere fills the society. A few people with righteousness are sometimes excluded and flow into negativity, and society falls into an incurable state. This situation can lead to the destruction of the country and the extinction of the race. (5) The general lack of national consciousness. The people of our country have always had too strong a personality. The so-called each person sweeps the snow in front of his own door and does not care about the frost on the roof of others. This kind of thinking has almost become a second nature. The general public rarely cares about the future of the country and even considers it noble not to ask about state affairs. Therefore, when they encounter national humiliation, they occasionally show their emotions and soon forget about it. There are so many national humiliation commemoration days in recent years, but the shame has not been erased after all. This cannot but be blamed on our own lack of effort, that is, the lack of national consciousness. The above points are really very serious ills in the current society, and they have a linked relationship. It is definitely not a short time to reverse them, nor can the thoughts and talents of a few people do it. It is necessary for the entire nation to rise up and start a grand reform movement. However, if we look at China, there are indeed not many people who have morality, talent, and a sense of responsibility. Those who have no morality are corrupt, those who are evil are becoming more evil, those who change their minds are changing their minds, and those who fall are falling. We don't need to talk about them. Even those who have morality and talent are often irresponsible, or they sing high-sounding tunes and scold others, or they have a sudden impulse today and a sudden impulse tomorrow, and in the end, they achieve nothing. As for those who have morality and talent and can really take responsibility, because there are too few talents in society, all things are concentrated on one person, and they have to do everything themselves from morning to night. They can only cope with the present and have very little time to think about things in the big, distant, and deep places. In this situation, it is not easy to remedy the current decadent situation. In the future, the government will have to make special efforts, and at the same time, it hopes that all compatriots in the country will have a common awareness to fight to save China."

何鍵 Recaptures Changsha

The Tragic Scene of Communist Bandits Slaughtering the People

Changsha Dispatch: Communist bandit leader Peng Dehuai, claiming to be the commander-in-chief of the 3rd Army Group of the Red Army, gathered over ten thousand communist bandits from Pingxiang and Liuyang. On the evening of the 27th of last month, they captured Changsha, engaging in burning, killing, and looting for ten days. Public and private losses amounted to tens of millions. Half the population has fled. Changsha, once considered the safest place by people from surrounding counties, is no longer a suitable place to live. It is feared that even ten years of recovery will not restore it to its original state. A brief account of the devastation caused by the communist bandits is as follows:

On the night of the 27th, at midnight, the 4th Route Army troops stationed in the city, along with the water and land police and local militia, completely retreated. Officials from various agencies, leaders of various organizations, personnel from the party headquarters, teachers and staff from various schools, and wealthy merchants all fled towards the west gate. All large steamers, whether heading downstream to Hankou or upstream to Xiangtan and Hengzhou, were packed to the brim with no room to stand. Even small private boats were fully hired. The cost of crossing the river was as high as one yuan per person, indicating the dire situation. Before the 4th Route Army had completely retreated, the communist bandit spear teams charged into the city. Initially, they only collected scattered firearms from the army, attacking the headquarters of the 4th Route Army, the provincial government, and various military and police agencies. Around 11 o'clock, the provincial government, the headquarters of the 4th Route Army, the anti-bandit headquarters, the Public Security Bureau, the garrison headquarters, the 15th Division headquarters, and the Changsha County government were all set on fire, burning throughout the night without stopping. On the 28th, they continued to burn civilian property, including the four major public buildings: Education Hall, Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall, Sun Yat-sen Library, Sun Yat-sen Museum, the Provincial Education Association, the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the County Party Headquarters, police stations in various districts, the Changyue Customs Supervisory Office, the Provincial Bank, the High Court, the District Court, the prison, the municipal preparatory office, the Army Survey Bureau, the Stamp Tax Bureau, the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau, and schools such as the Provincial First Normal School. Other buildings were demolished at the request of residents to avoid being affected, including various churches and church buildings inside and outside the city. The residences of important figures such as He Jian, Cao Dianqiu (member of the provincial government), Dai Douyuan (deputy commander of the 16th Division), Liu Yuezhi (secretary of the Provincial Party Committee), and Zhao Heng (president of the Provincial Bank), as well as dozens of private houses including the residence of Chen Peicheng, the general manager of Hunan Electric Light Company, were burned down. All large mansions and residences of important figures were led into by local hooligans and thugs. The Red Army (communist bandits with guns) and the Red Guards (communist bandits without guns wielding spears) broke down doors to search for so-called local tyrants, evil gentry, bureaucrats, military officers, party members, and reactionaries. The life or death of a person was determined by a single word from a passerby or a bystander hooligan. There was no trial or announcement of charges. Sometimes, people were directly sent to the bandit headquarters or the Soviet Provincial government for interrogation. Whenever they entered a people's residence, the Red Army and Red Guards first looted gold jewelry and silver money, and then incited hooligans and thugs to enter and carry away furniture, clothing, and other bulky items, showing favor to the proletariat. Sometimes, they would accuse hooligans and thugs of arbitrary looting and then shoot them, demonstrating their manipulation of the proletariat. On the 29th, Peng Dehuai arrived in Changsha and simultaneously established the so-called Hunan Provincial Soviet, appointing Li Lisan as chairman. He ordered the Changsha Chamber of Commerce to convene merchants from various industries to raise 700,000 yuan in cash within three days to ensure the protection of businesses, otherwise, they would take "free action." At that time, the bandit army was capturing people from various shops and extorting donations. Li Wenyu, Tongfeng, Tongzhen three gold shops, Huafeng, Rixin and other silk shops had already been broken into and looted by the bandit army, each suffering losses of tens of thousands. Only Yu Taihua Gold Shop paid 80,000 yuan in donations and was spared intrusion. Other large businesses had their owners and managers captured, and those identified as local tyrants were arrested. The whole city was filled with fear. The merchants had no choice but to nominate representatives to request that they be allowed to pay the full 700,000 yuan in cash and stop direct action against the merchants. The bandit army then turned to offering rewards: 2,000 yuan for capturing He Jian, Liu Jianshu, Xu Kexiang, Tao Guang, and Wei Suzhong; 1,600 yuan for capturing Cao Bowen, Song Hegeng, and Chen Changzu of the Provincial Committee; 600 yuan for capturing Feng Ti and others of the Party Committee, as well as Changsha County Magistrate Wang Zhengshi, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Hanchuan, Reformatory Director Zhou Anhan, and Water Police Captain Wang Guangqian. Half the reward would be given for bringing their heads. In addition, anyone who captured a Party Committee member, bureau chief, association president, or regiment commander would be rewarded with 200 yuan. Anyone who concealed information would have their entire family executed. Those who lived together and did not report would also have their entire family executed. As a result, over a thousand so-called local tyrants were arrested one after another and gathered outside Xiaowumen at the 49th Biao and the Bible School, the headquarters of Peng Dehuai. Those who donated several thousand or tens of thousands of yuan could be released, while the rest were arbitrarily executed. When the business community had paid the 700,000 yuan in cash, they were ordered to pay two months' worth of house rent, temporarily based on the assessed value of the houses, within two days. They obtained another 500,000 yuan in cash. No one dared to delay even slightly. Meanwhile, a land policy was promulgated, and a General Anti-Counterfeiting Headquarters and a Confiscation Committee were established, scheduled to begin a house-by-house general inspection and massacre on August 10th. Anyone hiding party members, public officials, military officers, or so-called reactionaries and local tyrants would be executed without mercy. Finding long gowns was considered proof of being a local tyrant's residence. Finding Western suits and school uniforms was considered proof of being a party member or public official's residence, and they would be executed without mercy. It was also planned to select ten men and women from each regiment to serve in the military, and all merchants and workers of various industries were ordered to establish associations and obtain membership certificates before the 8th. Anyone without a membership certificate would be placed under surveillance. Their intention was to communize all industries, merchants, and workers to expand their bandit forces. Therefore, the people of the whole city were terrified. The land and water transportation was sealed off on all sides, making it difficult to escape. Many people were publicly executed by the Red bandits on the street, including Army Hospital Director Liu Fucha, 4th Route Army Staff Officer Su Guangjun, Seal Keeper He Qingyun, County Party Committee member Jiang Xilong, and many others. More than a thousand people were executed outside the 49th Biao and Liuyangmen. The most dangerous thing was that the communist bandits set the price of one Sheng of rice at 200 Wen, one Jin of oil at 800 Wen, and one Jin of salt at 600 Wen. The general public took the opportunity to squeeze and buy. Because of the large number of people and the confusion, some did not pay and freely grabbed what they could. Therefore, within three days, all the rice, oil, and salt stores in the whole city were emptied, resulting in no goods available despite having money. The whole city was on the verge of starvation. People bought ash noodles to stave off hunger, resulting in the 40,000 bags of ash noodles stored in the ash noodle company outside the north gate being snatched away within half a day. The factory buildings were also demolished. Foreign companies also suffered losses, including the Jardine Matheson Company's warehouse and the Japanese Xiaoling Foreign Company. The people of the whole city were in this abyss of misery, unable to escape, and eagerly awaited the arrival of the army. On the morning of the 5th, at 3:00 AM, He Jian personally accompanied Tao Guang, commander of the 31st Division, and led the entire division from the Yiyang Ningxiang line to the west bank of the river to attack Changsha. He ordered Wang Dongyuan's brigade of the 15th Division to advance from Yuezhou Xiangyin to attack the north of Changsha. The three units of Liu Jianshu, commander of the 19th Division, Luo Fanying, commander of the 16th Division, and Chen Guangzhong, commander of the Independent 7th Brigade, concentrated in Tanli and advanced towards the south of Changsha and Liuyang. At the same time, he telegraphed the Hubei army under Luo Lin to assist in the attack on Changsha along the Xiang-E Railway and telegraphed the Jiangxi army under Zhang Huizan to block Pingxiang and Liuyang. Starting at 3:00 AM on the 5th, all troops were mobilized, with the local militias from Changning and Yiyiang counties advancing to the opposite bank of Changsha and feigning an attack on the west gate of the provincial capital. Wang Dongyuan's brigade of the 15th Division and Lei Jun's regiment, in coordination with Chen Wo's brigade of the 31st Division, forcibly crossed the river from Sancha Ji, 15 miles downstream of Changsha, and attacked the north gate and Xiaowumen 49th Biao of Changsha. Yan Zhongru's brigade of the 31st Division crossed the Jinjiang River upstream of Changsha and attacked the south gate of Changsha, Liuyangmen, and the Bible School outside Xiaowumen. Zhou Xiwu's brigade of the 31st Division crossed the Yuelu Mountain and attacked Lingguan Ferry and the south gate. The navy's Xianning and Yongsheng ships also fired their cannons to assist. At the same time, they agreed with Liu Luo and other divisions to attack Yiji湾 and Datuo铺 from both sides. At that time, most of the bandit army tended to heavily defend the Yijiawan Xiangtan line, and there were not many bandit troops in the province. Although they resisted fiercely, they were finally defeated due to the brave encirclement and attack of Tao's division and Wang's brigade. After five hours of stalemate, the bandits' headquarters was broken, more than 2,000 bandits were killed, and more than 1,000 male and female bandits were captured. Bandit Chairman Li Lisan and Bandit Political Department Director Yuan Guoping were killed. Only Peng Dehuai was wounded and broke through the encirclement and fled in a panic towards Huanghua City, Liuyang. After Peng fled, the remaining bandits were successively annihilated. By about 9:00 AM, the whole city was cleared. Only twenty or so people were accidentally injured. Tao Guang personally supervised the division to pursue the bandits. On the 6th, He Jian crossed the river from the spinning factory and returned to the province, temporarily working in the YMCA building. On the 7th, division commanders Liu Jianshu, Luo Fanying, and Wei Suzhong, deputy division commanders Luo Shujia and Dai Douyuan, and Chen Guangzhong and other independent brigade commanders led their troops to the province and ordered their troops to encircle and attack Pingxiang and Liuyang. Provincial government members Zeng Jiwu, Cao Bowen, Cao Dianzhu, and Zhang Kailian, and Secretary-General Yi Shuzhu returned to the province from Xiangxiang, Hengzhou, and Hankou. The departments of the 4th Route Army headquarters and the Anti-Bandit Headquarters moved from Xiangtan to the province and temporarily worked in the YMCA. Wang Dongyuan, brigade commander, was appointed as the garrison commander of the provincial capital. Starting on the 8th, the entire city was cut off from transportation to search for communist bandits hiding and the thugs who aided them, and to search for the public and private property that was looted to clear bandit traces. All follow-up measures and anti-bandit strategies were decided at a joint military-political meeting on the 8th to resolve everything. It is reported that He Jian has made up his mind to destroy Peng's bandit lair to eliminate future troubles and thank the people of Hunan. (August 7th)

Jinan Suffers Severe Rain Disaster

Streets and Alleys Become Waterlands

Weather Turns Suddenly Cold

Jinan Dispatch: Jinan and its surrounding areas have experienced a sudden heavy rainfall in recent days. Since the 2nd of this month, it has been raining for five days. Although there have been occasional clearings, it has quickly turned cloudy and rainy again. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the rain was particularly heavy, pouring down like a waterfall. In the afternoon, a strong wind rose again, and the wind and rain mixed together. The weather changed abruptly and turned cold. Many people changed into lined clothing. The streets and roads of the city were a vast expanse of water. In low-lying areas, the water was as deep as two or three feet, and the current was very swift, carrying mud and sand. Therefore, traffic on the streets was cut off. Cars passing through splashed water, resembling boats on a river. Most of the old houses in various places collapsed, and many of the newly built houses also leaked. The areas outside Linxiang Gate, inside the North Gate, at the South City Wall, and at the East City Wall were particularly severely affected. Some residents moved to the city walls to take temporary shelter. The water in the Xiaoqing River between the Dongliushui Rainbow Bridge also rose above the bank by more than two feet. The shops on the main roads, due to their low-lying location, all used burlap sacks filled with soil to place in front of their doors to prevent water from entering. Those who did not prepare in time suffered from the rain, and the water inside the houses was also several feet deep. The rain began to ease slightly at 10:00 PM, and the accumulated water on the roads gradually receded, but the stones were exposed and the roads were rugged and difficult to travel. Unexpectedly, the rain intensified again after 12:00 AM and continued until this morning (6th), and it is still cloudy and rainy. The north wind suddenly rose, and it felt like entering late autumn. Even in lined clothes, it still felt cold. Many young children were already wearing cotton clothes. Such a situation has not been seen in recent years. (August 6th)

Communist Bandits Plot to Disturb Harbin Unsuccessful

Han Shouben Orchestrates from Within

Harbin Dispatch: The local Communist Party planned to carry out disturbances on August 1st, first attacking the headquarters of the 18th Brigade to seize weapons, and then attacking the Special Region Administrative Chief's Office, the Road Police Department, the Public Security Bureau, and the Special Police Management Office. Their plan of attack was to incite the troops of the 18th Brigade and 26th Brigade stationed in the area, and to collude with the 36th Shed Chinese workers of the Eastern Railway. On July 30th, after the Chinese workers of the Eastern Railway were dismissed, the workers still lingered and did not leave the venue.

Page 8

Someone noticed that the workers were preparing knives, axes, and other weapons, which were sharpened very sharply. They secretly reported to the road police. The road police secretly arrested one or two workers and interrogated them. After confirming the truth, they immediately notified the military and police agencies responsible to strengthen their guard. Therefore, the incident on August 1st did not occur. However, the Special Police Department discovered in recent days that the main figure planning this event was Han Shouben, a former reporter for the Changchun Dadong Daily. Han had served as a special commissioner of the Jilin Central Party Affairs Department during the secret work of the Eastern Province Party Affairs. After the purge of the communists, Han lost his position and worked as a reporter for the Changchun Dadong Daily, secretly promoting communism for the Third International and actively contacting student circles. Last spring, he was discovered by Huo Zhanyi, the president of the Dadong Daily, and was fired from the company. Han went to the Harbin area to engage in activities and was promoted to serve as the secretary of the Eastern Railway Industrial Maintenance Association, provoking labor unrest and promoting communism. After being noticed by the authorities, he voluntarily resigned and returned to Changchun to serve as a teacher at the Seventh Middle School in the Special Region. He was again discovered by the principal for promoting communism at the school and was dismissed. Recently, after the fall of Changsha, the Communist Party in various places was eager to move. Han claimed to be a representative of Song Zheyuan's Northwest Army and publicly engaged in activities. Subsequently, he was discovered by the authorities and arrested by the special police in a inn on Daoli Street on the 5th of this month. That night, he was escorted to Liaoning by one inspector, one translator, and two judicial police officers. However, on the way, near the Laoshaogou Station between Harbin and Changchun, it is unknown what tricks Han used, but he escaped from the car under the strict supervision of the crowd. The police officers who were escorting him returned to Harbin and reported to the authorities. Suspecting that they were selling him out, they have been all arrested and imprisoned. It is generally said that after Han's escape, the communist disaster in the Eastern Province may break out sooner or later. (6th)

Japanese Police's Brutality in Yanbian

Japanese Intend to Invade and Occupy Yanbian

Japanese Police Actually Assault Our Military Officers

Yanbian Circles Blood-Written Declaration

Harbin Correspondence

In recent years, Japanese and Korean people have been migrating to the various districts of Jidong Yanbian in increasing numbers, becoming the masters instead of the guests, and making the guest room the master's hall, directly causing the status of the nationals of the sovereign country to be reversed with that of the expatriate residents. It is reported that as of the beginning of May of this year, in the various counties under the jurisdiction of Yanji alone, there were as many as 1.3 million Japanese and Korean expatriates, while the number of Chinese people was very small. Therefore, Japanese and Korean vagrants often take advantage of opportunities to bully the Chinese people. The Japanese government offices in Yanbian have been established everywhere without our permission, and when incidents occur, they stir up trouble to protect them, causing the Chinese people to suffer immensely. There have been numerous cases of Japanese and Korean people killing Chinese people and oppressing our government offices, and official negotiations have been endless and without thorough solutions. Seeing our weakness, the Japanese have increased their bullying day by day. On July 28th, there was another incident of assaulting our military officers. After this incident occurred, the people of several counties in Yanbian, without prior consultation, informed each other and immediately formed a powerful organization to hold a meeting to assist the government officials and vowed to confront the situation to the death. On the day of the meeting, some people bit their fingers and wrote a letter in blood, drafting a declaration to announce to all circles in the country, requesting unanimous support. Recently, the Jilin Provincial Authorities have telegraphed Zhang Shuhan, the negotiator in Yanji, to investigate and report back, and to handle the matter carefully before the provincial order arrives to avoid triggering major changes. The declaration is recorded as follows: "Jilin Yanji Longjing Village is an important town on the Chinese Yanbian border. Japan calls it Jiandao, revealing its intention to annex it. A Japanese Consulate General has been specially established, with branch offices in Yanhun and Wangqing. More than 400 armed police officers have also been forcibly set up, ostensibly to protect expatriates, but in reality, they are carrying out aggression. In recent years, they have destroyed our customs, forcibly built railways, interfered in our administration, poisoned our people, and sent armed police officers to arrest people without cause, acting arrogantly and recklessly in all kinds of barbaric ways. Recently, on July 28th, the 1st Battalion of the 7th Regiment of the 13th Brigade of the local garrison army learned that some Korean civilians were gathering to gamble and extort money. The garrison army sent Zhang Fengquan, the second company commander, along with three plainclothes soldiers to arrest them. Three gambling offenders were caught on the spot and were about to be taken back to the company for interrogation. As they passed in front of the Japanese police station, the Japanese police suddenly interfered. Company Commander Zhang argued with them on the grounds of reason, but the Japanese police were unreasonable and did not listen. They summoned many Japanese police officers and beat Company Commander Zhang for a long time, and took him to the Japanese Consulate. Company Commander Zhang was wearing an army uniform, which was torn and tattered, and he was covered in bruises. There is a certificate from a British doctor as evidence. The facts are clear. The Japanese police officers and consuls are still trying to defend themselves with a hundred excuses. The local people are angry and agitated and vowed not to live with the Japanese police. When the municipal people's congress was convened, the masses bit their fingers and wrote blood letters. They have unanimously decided to protest seriously to the Japanese side, demanding the withdrawal of the Japanese police in Yanbian, the punishment of senior Japanese police officers and the Japanese police officers who caused the incident, and a formal apology to our country in order to uphold the national system and maintain sovereignty. The border people vow to resist unanimously to the death. Therefore, we present this statement in blood and respectfully hope for your attention. Jilin Yanji County Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Student Joint Association." (August 6th)

Sales of Dong Province Soybeans in Germany

Jilin Correspondence: The Eastern Province is a soybean-producing region, and also the only major exporter. However, agricultural production and commercial transport are both lacking in improvement and are gradually declining, resulting in many obstacles in sales to various parts of Europe. Recently, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has forwarded a letter from the German Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai, stating the situation of Dong Province soybean sales in Germany in recent years, as it is related to Dong Province's foreign trade. The original letter was copied and sent to the Jilin Provincial Government for investigation, and then forwarded to the Jilin Chamber of Commerce Federation for study. The original letter is extracted below to show that Dong Province soybeans have a considerable position in Germany.

(I) Soybeans in Germany

Are purely used for various industries and oil mill enterprises. Soybean oil is used for food and industrial needs. Crushed soybeans are now regarded as the most nutritious feed for livestock, as it is known that feeding cattle with it can increase milk production. The use of soybean flour can also be substituted for other common flours, and it can increase the nutritional quality of bread.

(II) The demand and consumption of soybean oil and other soybean products in Germany are flourishing. The use of soybean oil is particularly important for supplying nutrients. Crushed soybeans are now regarded as the most valuable food.

(III) Crushed soybeans can be substituted for oily seed products such as coconut cakes and peanut cakes. As for soybeans, there is nothing else that can directly replace them.

(IV) According to current news, there is no possibility of a decline in soybeans in Germany this year. The number of imports in the first three months of this year already exceeds that of last year. As for the decline in prices, it is not due to weak demand, but due to the common decline in the prices of agricultural products worldwide. This common decline in the prices of agricultural products will inevitably lead to a sharp reduction in the purchasing power of German farmers and a corresponding reduction in the need for livestock consumption. However, when the above-mentioned prices are low, the demand for soybeans by German farmers still increases.

(V) The number of soybean imports in the past five years is listed below to show the increase in Germany's need for this item:

1925: 336,000 tons

1926: 370,038 tons

1927: 576,096 tons

1928: 847,724 tons

1929: 1,023,858 tons

1930: January to March: 291,715 tons

Germany imports several times more from China than it exports to China. It should be noted that the value of exports to China in 1929 was 190 million gold marks, while the value of imports from China was 365 million gold marks.

Jiangsu Province Government Expenses Temporarily Issued at 50%

Limited to August and September

Supplementary Issue After October

Chen Qicai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department, previously submitted a request to the Provincial Government Committee for discussion on measures due to heavy military spending and financial difficulties. After the 319th meeting of the Provincial Government, three measures were decided: (1) Military police supplies and education subsidies will be issued as usual. (2) The expenses of various agencies will be issued at 50% first, and the agencies will allocate them themselves, temporarily limited to August and September. Supplementary issues will be made successively after October. (3) Other expenses that can be issued later will be determined by the responsible agency and reported to the meeting. The Provincial Government has already issued separate orders to the various departments and associations to follow the procedures and has issued instructions from the Finance Department to the county governments and county finance bureaus to comply with the procedures.

Cracking Down on Shanghai Kidnapping Bandit Criminals

The neighbor of the Maitreya Temple on Nanchengdu Road, Shanghai, Mr. Liu, the owner of the Liu Mansion, who works at the Gold Exchange, was kidnapped by bandits last month and demanded 50,000 yuan for ransom. After the family members of the victim received several letters, they commissioned someone to negotiate the ransom at the bandit den. After several negotiations, the business was redeemed. Afterwards, a tipster reported to Detective Cao of the Police Department that Yu Baoren, a driver of the Xinglong Auto Company on Disiwei Road, was also involved in the Liu case. Yu has now abandoned his job and is hiding in Suzhou's Sand Skin Lane, Henglong Lane, Kaijia Lane No. 4 in Changmen with his relatives. After receiving the report, Detective Cao informed the Police Department on the former (10th) day and brought official documents, accompanied by the tipster to Suzhou, and discussed the arrest measures with Xu Fengshan, the detective captain of the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau. At about 7:00 AM yesterday morning, Detective Xu, along with detectives Shao Henglong and Qu Jinsheng, accompanied Detective Cao Ashan and the tipster of the Police Department to Kaijia Lane No. 4 secretly, and arrested Yu Baoren. He was immediately taken to the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau for custody. Detective Cao returned to Shanghai at noon with the tipster and reported to the Police Department. It was decided that an official document would be prepared and sent to Suzhou today (12th) to welcome the extradition and handle the case. It was also heard that Mr. Liu was also kidnapped last year and redeemed for 30,000.

Suicide Case at Changguang Bridge

Zhang Bairong (36 years old) from Huashu, Jiangyin County, came to Wuxi with his wife, Ms. Xu (named Ruizhen), a few months ago to seek a livelihood due to financial difficulties. Unexpectedly, an old woman named Granny Yang, who lived on Tonghui Road (Granny Yang specializes in selling women), acted as an intermediary and sold Ms. Xu to Zhang Jiren, the owner of Jiuchengchang Cigarette and Paper Shop outside Guangfu Gate on Wanqian Road, as his wife for 60 yuan. Ms. Xu received 40 yuan, and Granny Yang received 20 yuan. When Bairong came to Wuxi for the second time, he learned the truth. Overwhelmed with shame and anger, he had thoughts of ending his life. He wrote a suicide note at the First Hotel on Malu Wudong yesterday and secretly went to Changguang Bridge at Huangnitou in Guangqin District and threw himself into the river. Around 4 PM, Jin A’mei, the chief of the 17th Tu of that area, discovered the incident and immediately reported it to the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. The bureau dispatched police officer Xia Zixuan to investigate. As a result, a discarded package of green willow twigs, a short shirt, and a suicide note signed by Zhang Bairong were found on the ground. The officers from the Sixth Branch searched for a long time but did not find Zhang's body. They took the belongings and suicide note back to the bureau to be filed for further investigation. It is also heard that Zhang Jiren, knowing the situation was bad after the incident, had already fled elsewhere with Zhang Xu.

Appeal Judgement in Frame-up Case

Fei Zhongliang, the Deputy Township Head, and Qin Xifang, both from Xishan Township, Kaiyuan Township, Fourth District, were previously accused by Gao Zhongyu, a resident of the township, of reporting to the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau that a meeting he convened in the township had counter-revolutionary implications, resulting in a frame-up. Subsequently, the county government sentenced Qin Xifang to six months in prison and Fei Zhongliang to two months in prison. Qin and others, dissatisfied with the verdict, hired lawyer An Ruotai to appeal to the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court summoned both parties to court for interrogation the day before yesterday. After two hours of debate, the verdict was announced yesterday, acquitting Qin Xifang and upholding the original sentence for Fei Zhongliang. However, Gao Zhongyu declared in court that he was dissatisfied and would appeal to the Supreme Court.

Yangzhou

A Glimpse of Yangzhou's City Closure and Market Strike

According to Mr. Wu, who came from Yangzhou to Shanghai, around 10 PM on the 9th of this month, gunshots suddenly rang out in the bustling Yuanmen Bridge and Duozi Street areas, along with a great commotion. Silence was restored after about two hours. It was later learned that the reason was that an injured soldier had caused trouble at the Yangzhou Bathhouse, which was still under construction on Sucang Street, that afternoon. The person in charge offered six yuan to settle the matter, but it did not satisfy the soldier. He then gathered more people to cause trouble, but was unsuccessful. He then gathered two or three hundred people, distributed them, and began to retaliate. After entering the city, they first seized the firearms of the merchant corps guarding the posts at Yuanmen Bridge and other places, wielding iron bars and, in some cases, fast-firing guns. Fortunately, the merchant corps was well-trained and fought bravely. Only Xiong Xiaoyun and Guo Jufu lost one gun each. Dan Wenyi was injured, but his gun was not lost. However, Ju Zheng Guo, the guard at Yuanmen Bridge, was struck on the head with an iron bar, causing blood to flow, but he was able to hold his gun and break through the siege. He fell several steps away and fired at one of the injured soldiers chasing him, and the crowd scattered. Xie Chaobin, the Chief of Staff of the 133rd Brigade and the Chief of the Joint Military-Police Inspection Office, heard the alarm and led a team on patrol. At Xiaodongmen Longtou Pass, they encountered the perpetrators, who opened fire on them. The crowd retreated, and Xie led the team in pursuit. Most of the perpetrators exited through the South Gate, while the rest scattered. During the disturbance, all the stores in the city were closed, and the city gates were also closed. It was heard that after the Chamber of Commerce and the Brigade Headquarters held a meeting, more soldiers and police were dispatched to the Fortune Gate to open one gate.

Man Killed with a Punch Due to a Jesting Remark

Lin Chun, the second son of Tao Jincheng of Huangtang Bridge, Section Two, Qishan Township, Dongwai, was working as a tenant farmer at the Xu family in Qingyangxia Village. The night before last (the 9th), he went home, and his cousin Zibao invited him to eat a late Mid-Year Festival meal. After the meal, Lin Chun saw Zibao's family propping up the door to cool off and jokingly remarked, "Is propping up the door for dead people to sleep?" Zibao, misunderstanding his words, punched Lin Chun in the heart. Lin Chun fell to the ground and died instantly. Later, his mother and wife cried foul. The Public Security Bureau reported to the county for an examination, but the murderer had already fled. Yesterday afternoon, relatives intervened and resolved the matter peacefully.

They only eat two meals of sweet potato dried per day. The day before yesterday, more than fifty hostages angered the bandits and were all shot and their bodies thrown into the sea. Bandit troops were discovered at Wuxing Port in Funing County. After being repelled by Commander Deng of the 265th Regiment of the 133rd National Revolutionary Army and Police Captain Xiong, they reoccupied the Zhaowangjian, Daxingzhen, and Nandoukan areas. Zhang, the manager of the Huacheng Company, was kidnapped and a ransom of 100,000 yuan was demanded. The firearms of the Hede Company were also robbed. All the places they passed were disrupted and harmed. Local bandits seized the opportunity to rise up like bees, robbing, kidnapping, and killing every day. The people are living in misery. The National Revolutionary Army has temporarily been transferred back to Funing City. The Wuxing Port defense line has ordered Police Captain Huang to lead troops to block and defend it.

Zhu Ruifeng Arrested, Dongkan Strikes

Zhu Ruifeng's house, the head of the Dongkan Red Cross Branch, was suddenly surrounded by about twenty people who looked like soldiers at 4 AM on July 29th. They broke down the gate, jumped over the wall, and immediately arrested Zhu Huanwen, Zhu Ruifeng's elder brother, and looted all the valuables in the house, incurring losses estimated at about 30,000 yuan. They then took a boat and bound them away. As a result, all the stores in the town closed, and the people were fearful. Telegrams were sent to the National Government, the Department of Civil Affairs, and the Shanghai Red Cross Headquarters, requesting assistance. It has been three days, and the stores in Dongkan have not yet resumed business.

Jiashan

Fei Xu Kidnapped

Fei Xu, a widowed farm woman from Chenjiaham, North Township, Taozhuang in the county, worked for the Hu family in Wujiang for thirty years and had accumulated some savings. Last spring, she returned home to renovate her old house. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 4th of this month, bandits suddenly came to extort 1,000 yuan. Eventually, they agreed to 250 yuan. Both sides agreed to pay the money at dusk on the 9th. Ms. Xu gathered the money, and on the night of the 9th, the bandits came to collect the money and left. Unexpectedly, the next morning, the bandits came again, claiming that the money had not been received. They tied up Ms. Xu, beat her, and burned her lower body before taking her away. Around the 11th, after arranging 500 yuan, they were allowed to redeem her. They also forced the neighboring neighbors to be guarantors. If the family of Fei Xu concealed any information, the neighbors would be questioned and burned.

Pinghu

Threatening Letters One After Another

Wang Xingqing and Wang Wujin, farmers in Xianfeng Temple, about three miles from Quan Gongting, received two threatening letters on the 2nd and 4th of this month, demanding 1,000 yuan. The Wang brothers ignored them. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 6th, more than twenty bandits, wearing white headbands and carrying firearms, swarmed into the Wang family's house, tied up Xingqing and Wujin, and hung them up, demanding that they pay the money. Wang claimed he had no money, so the bandits beat them. After Xingqing's wife knelt down and pleaded, they agreed to pay 1,000 yuan on the 10th and wrote a promissory note. Only then did the bandits leave. Xu Heshang, Liu A'san, and Zhou Sanzun in the village also received threatening letters demanding 5,000 yuan.

Huzhou

Bandit Robbery, Victim Wounded

Cai Wanrong, a farmer near Dama Town, Deqing County, Huzhou, worked diligently and had a prosperous family. At midnight on the 6th, six bandits with mixed accents and short knives and wooden clubs broke into his house. Cai Wanrong saw that the bandits did not have firearms and tried to resist, but he was outnumbered and wounded by the bandits' knives and clubs. One bandit guarded Wanrong while the remaining bandits entered the house and ransacked all the clothes, silver, and other items. After the incident, Cai's family hired a doctor to treat him.

Woman Murders Biological Son Due to Affair

Madam, the wife of the late Wang Zhineng, the owner of Wang Tongchang's bronze and tin shop in Dongzha, Nanxun, is over forty years old and has a lewd nature. After Zhineng's death, Madam had an affair with her husband's nephew, Mr. Jia, and they soon lived together as if they were husband and wife. Zhineng had a son named Wubao, who is now eighteen years old. Two years ago, he married a woman surnamed Mou, and they lived in harmony. However, Madam, deeply afraid that this would be detrimental to herself, incited him from within, falsely accusing her daughter-in-law of misconduct. Wubao was young and ignorant, so he was confused and began to mistreat her. Last year, she was once again severely reprimanded. Later, the woman suddenly disappeared and has not been heard from since. The night before last, Madam colluded with her lover and planned to murder her son, Wubao, with a bayonet. Fortunately, the neighbors on the left and right were not yet asleep and heard a scream. They rushed to rescue him, and Wubao escaped from the tiger's mouth and was not stabbed to death. The neighbors arrested the adulterer and adulteress and sent them to the Public Security Bureau of the town for legal proceedings.

Shangyu

Continued Record of Fan Shoukang's Escape

Since Mr. Fan Shoukang, the former principal of Chunhui, escaped danger, visitors have been flocking to his door every day. Here is an excerpt from his conversation, which was not fully reported earlier: When I was kidnapped and taken by the bandits in the dark, I fell more than thirty times on the narrow and dilapidated streets. When passing the Wu Zixu Temple, I accidentally fell into a muddy field. When the bandits helped me up, my shoes were gone. I ran barefoot on the sandy and rocky road for more than an hour. My soles were blistered, and I could barely stand. Then the bandits gave me cloth shoes to wear before I reached the place where I was imprisoned. There were four bandits guarding me. Every afternoon, one bandit would go out and return with a bucket of corn to feed me. Aside from occasionally making pointless consolations, someone from Shanghai would come here every other day. These people were extremely secretive and had been trained. I heard from one of them that their party members were all over Yuyin, Yu, Ci, Xin, Sheng, Fenghua, and other counties, numbering about one division or more. I also heard that the Chunzhong Nursing School Sports Committee planned to celebrate the success of the escort and the escape of the former principal at the beginning of the semester.

Another Case of Smuggling Rice Out of the Territory

After the Kang Rice Company outside the East Gate caused public outrage among the people by smuggling early rice out of the territory, unfortunately, a similar incident occurred in Songxia Town in Yuxi, Shangyu. Here is a record of the incident: A few days ago, the Zhou Yihe Rice Shop colluded with a Shaoxing rice dealer nicknamed "Nun" to transport 500 dan of rice in batches by boat out of the territory. Unexpectedly, when passing through the Tan Village of Li Hai Suo and Xiajia bu, it was discovered by the villagers of Qianzhuang Quzui, who rang gongs and gathered a crowd to cross the river to chase them. Two small boats were intercepted, containing a total of more than 100 shi of rice. The rest had already been transported away. The boats, rice, boatmen, and rice dealers were all detained and reported to the village committee, the Public Security Bureau, and other agencies. Two meetings were held at the Sixth Community and the Five Dragon Temple, attended by more than 1,000 people. It was decided to detain the rice dealer, Nun, and hand her over to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The fourteen bags of rice that had not yet been transported were also detained. Later, Yu Yantang and others came forward to mediate the results. The rice dealer, Nun, was released, fined one hundred yuan, forty yuan to be used for the repair of the Five Dragon Temple, and sixty yuan to be allocated to the Fifth District Office. The detained rice was returned in full. The Zhou Yi Tai was leniently exempted from further investigation. Afterward, the people there decided on two measures: (1) Strictly prohibit rice merchants from hoarding; (2) If the above situation is found in the future, the confiscated rice will be confiscated, and the informant will be rewarded with three yuan per bag.

Letter

Letter from Refugees from Hengfeng, Shangrao, Fleeing to Zhejiang

Hengfeng, Shangrao, is located in the central part of eastern Jiangxi. The land is barren and the people are poor. Years of wind, drought, water, and insect plagues have occurred repeatedly. How can we bear this? Since the rampage of the Communist bandits led by Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, etc., under the name of the Third International, organized the Soviet puppet government, inciting workers and peasants and anesthetizing the youth, their red flames are more ferocious than floods and beasts. The areas bordering the northwest townships of Hengfeng in Shangrao are particularly close, and therefore, they were the first to be incited. Rumors spread, and people were startled every night, making it difficult for them to sleep. For two years now, the tens of thousands of people in the county have been living in deep water. Since Hengfeng was disturbed and occupied by the Communist bandits, the number of refugees displaced has reached thousands, all of whom have taken refuge in Shangrao City. On February 23rd of this year, Shangrao County was suddenly attacked and occupied by the Fang bandits. The county office and the court were burned down, and most of the shops and residences were looted. More than twenty people were kidnapped, and the loss of property and materials was estimated at more than 200,000 yuan. Fortunately, the county was recaptured in just a few hours, and the refugees were spared from being searched and killed. Unexpectedly, the bandit nests were not destroyed, and there was no large army to suppress them. The bandit forces were rampant and became increasingly severe. The area within ten miles of the city had become a bandit area. At dawn on July 24th, Shangrao County was once again attacked and occupied by the Fang bandits, who gathered a puppet Red Army and peasant bandits numbering about 20,000, with more than 3,000 guns, knives, and spears. From the 24th when they entered the city to the afternoon of the 28th, after the bandits learned of the news of the joint counterattack by various counties, they led their troops to withdraw, occupying the city for four days, searching, burning, killing, and looting from house to house, even worse than before. The exact number of shops and residences looted is unknown. More than 200 people were kidnapped. About 300 people were searched out and brutally killed by the bandits. Most of the shops and residences were destroyed, and property was looted. Corpses were lying all over the city, and the stench was unbearable. The refugees from Hengfeng and the northwest townships of Shangrao who were taking refuge in the city were regarded as counter-revolutionaries and were searched, arrested, and killed with particular cruelty. The refugees who were killed were beheaded, disemboweled, and their hearts dug out. The situation was so tragic that it was painful to even talk about. The loss of property and materials in Shangrao in this tragic invasion by the Communist bandits was more than one million yuan. The essence of the county seat was destroyed without any remains. It was truly a tragedy unprecedented in recent centuries. Although the Communist bandits have retreated outside the city, the bandit area is approaching the county seat and could arrive at any moment. The refugees and others fear that they will come again, so they are helping the old and carrying the young. The number of those who gathered reached more than 5,000. First, they fled to Yushan, but because Yujing borders Shangrao, rumors abounded. The refugees were all fleeing from the gunshots and bullets of Shangrao City. Having just left the dangerous situation, they were like frightened birds, no longer protecting themselves. They fled from Yu to Zhejiang. Now, they are in Changshan, exposed to the wind and sleeping in the open, without clothes or food, looking up to their homeland. The fields and houses are no longer theirs. They have endured all the pain of displacement, with no tears to shed. Hengfeng has been tragically disturbed by the Communist bandits for four years, and the county seat has been occupied by the bandits for nearly a year. If there is no large army to suppress them, the tens of thousands of displaced people in the two counties will inevitably become starving corpses and take the risk of becoming bandits. If the government can show compassion and rescue them, it should quickly send a large army to station at the key locations of Shangrao and Hengfeng, order them to carry out the suppression, and set a deadline for the elimination of the bandits. At the same time, it should carry out a clearing of the countryside to eliminate the source of the bandits and eradicate the roots. Furthermore, the more than 5,000 refugees, helping the old and carrying the young, who are taking refuge in Changshan, Zhejiang, are all citizens of the country and our compatriots. They should be treated equally. We should quickly distribute grain to provide appropriate relief to maintain their livelihoods and not let them wait anxiously for their fate. The representatives of the refugees from Hengfeng and Shangrao counties taking refuge in Changshan, Zhejiang, Zeng Renmin, Wang Hengyuan, Fang Chengjun, and others, more than 5,000 people, together bow and request.

Local News

Shanghai County Government Receives Measures to Promote the National Calendar

A total of six items:

The Central Political Committee drafted the measures to promote the National Calendar. The National Government has now revised and promulgated them, and ordered all provinces to comply. Yesterday, the Shanghai County Government received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs, along with the measures to promote the National Calendar, as follows: (1) Move the New Year holidays and various ceremonies and entertainment of the abolished lunar calendar to the National Calendar New Year. (A) All people in various places should move the number of holidays for the abolished lunar calendar New Year and various ceremonies, entertainment, and decorations used before and after the abolished lunar calendar New Year, such as New Year greetings, group worship, ancestor worship, spring banquets, lantern viewing, tying color, pasting spring couplets, etc., to the National Calendar New Year. (B) Party and government agencies should actively implement and announce to the people in advance to comply. The abolished lunar calendar New Year is not allowed to be a holiday, and it is not allowed to take holidays under other names. (2) The dates of local market towns, fairs, and temple fairs should all comply with the National Calendar. (A) Party and government agencies should announce in advance that the dates of market towns, fairs, and temple fairs should all comply with the National Calendar dates and strictly prohibit the use of the abolished lunar calendar. (3) Correspondence and publications attached to the abolished lunar calendar are prohibited from being printed, transported, and sold. (A) Party and government agencies should strictly prohibit the private printing, transportation, and sale of abolished lunar calendar almanacs and publications attached to the abolished lunar calendar. Those who privately print, transport, and sell them will be severely punished according to law. (4) The farming season for farmers in various places should be calculated and instructed using the National Calendar. (A) Party and government agencies should send personnel to consult and discuss the National Calendar calculation methods for the farming season in various places based on the climate and soil conditions of each place, and compile and print explanatory brochures, charts, songs, etc., explaining the farming work for each season of the month and distribute them for implementation. (B) Governments at all levels should mark the twenty-four solar terms and farming work for each month on wooden signs and post them on thoroughfares and prosperous villages. Each district must set up at least four such signs to inform the public as a standard for sowing, transplanting, cultivating, and harvesting. (C) The Central Agricultural Extension Committee and the Agricultural Extension Committees of various provinces should pay special attention to the revision and instruction of the farming season using the National Calendar calculation. (D) The supplementary education for farmers and the primary school education in rural areas should pay attention to the instruction of the farming work for each month of the National Calendar, and incorporate such materials into textbooks so that farmers in various places can have a deep understanding of this. (E) When reprinting National Calendar almanacs in various places, they should consider adding materials on farming matters. (5) Print more National Calendar almanacs, day calendars, monthly calendars, etc., to promote implementation. (A) Compile and order them jointly by the Central Propaganda Department and the Astronomical Research Institute. (B) Print and distribute them by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education and stipulate the printing methods. (C) The Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education should jointly prepare a budget for the printing costs of the National Calendar almanacs and submit it to the National Government for review and order the Ministry of Finance to allocate funds accordingly. (6) It is stipulated that all business accounts, private contracts, and all documents and bookkeeping must use the National Calendar in order to have legal effect (implementation methods should be drafted by the competent authorities of the National Government).

Cai Pei Returns to Office After Leave

Discusses the Situation of Maintaining the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

Cai Ziping, the Director of the Navigation Administration Department dispatched by the Ministry of Communications to Shanghai to serve as acting managing director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, informed Minister Wang Boqun at the beginning of his tenure that he could only maintain the position for ten days and requested that the National Government appoint someone to take over. Last week, Cai requested leave to return to Beijing due to his wife's severe stroke and strongly resigned from his concurrent position to Minister Wang. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which was on the verge of collapse, suddenly appeared to be without a leader. The company's labor union sent a telegram to the ministry requesting maintenance, and Minister Wang urged Cai to quickly return to the office after his leave and to take on the difficult task. Cai, urged by Minister Wang, arrived in Shanghai on the Sunday night train and reported to the office yesterday to resume his duties as usual. The reporter made a special visit to ask about the future of the bureau, and he answered as follows:

Continues to Serve Concurrently

The reporter asked Cai whether he came to Shanghai this time to formally assume the position of managing director. Cai replied that he has always been indifferent to officialdom. He initially strongly declined the position of managing director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and only agreed to serve concurrently for ten days. Later, due to his wife's illness, he returned to Beijing to attend to his personal affairs. However, Minister Wang again urged him to return due to public and private considerations, so he came to the bureau again to continue serving as acting managing director. He has again requested the National Government to appoint someone. If the official personnel arrive at the bureau tomorrow, he will immediately hand over his duties and return to his original position in the Navigation Administration Department. Currently, the First Section is temporarily acting as the managing director, as he is determined not to hold this position of managing director.

Financial Problems

The most difficult point at present is the financial problem. The reporter asked about his plans for finance. Cai replied that as an acting official, he could not talk about plans. However, at this time, when the bureau is riddled with holes, he will do his best to raise some funds to pay the arrears of salaries to sailors and seamen so as not to hinder shipping. The arrears of salaries for the office staff in the bureau for several months are also being planned to be issued in some amount to maintain everyone's livelihood.

Tidying Up the Future

When a reporter inquired about tidying up the future, Cai [Yuanpei] replied that Zhao Tieqiao had been in charge for over two years but still failed to cure the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's (招商局) illness, and it was even worsening. Considering the current situation, the company's condition was not yet beyond salvation. If one could carefully research and find ways to reorganize, it was not impossible to revive it. However, as he was not a reorganization specialist, he need not add his opinions. When the National Government appoints a specialist, they will naturally have their own methods. For now, he was merely acting as a temporary substitute, and everything would proceed according to existing procedures, with each department responsible for its own work. He would primarily maintain the status quo. What he could firmly guarantee was that he would not allow shipping to be suspended for even a day while he was in office. This he could tell the reporter. The reporter then took his leave.

German Nationals Celebrate the Anniversary of the Establishment of the Constitution

Yesterday was the anniversary of the establishment of the German Constitution. Chen Shiguang, the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and representatives from various institutions attended. The host and guests happily dispersed around noon.

Establishment of the Bureau of Weights and Measures

Preparing to Implement a Publicity Plan

Inspection Work to Begin Soon

The Shanghai Bureau of Weights and Measures has been under preparation since the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau submitted a request to the Municipal Government to establish a preparatory office three months ago. During this time, matters such as examining and sending inspection personnel, implementing temporary surveys of weights and measures, convening workshops for various weights and measures manufacturing stores, compiling various promotional materials and commodity price conversion tables, etc., have all been completed. The staff sent to Beijing for training at the end of last month have also returned to the bureau one after another. Recently, the Social Affairs Bureau consulted with the Manufacturers of Flower and Tree of Xiejiao Guild to rent the guild's surplus rooms for the bureau's office. Construction and renovation of the building began immediately. Zhou Zanming, a staff member and technician of the bureau, was concurrently appointed as the director of the bureau to take charge of everything. Preparations are now complete and the bureau was officially established yesterday, operating at the new location. The first step of work, it is said, will be to implement the pre-determined publicity plan. As for the inspection work, it will begin after the revision and promulgation of the regulations on weights and measures equipment from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce.

Chongguang Talks About Negotiations Regarding the Changsha Incident

Demanding Compensation for Damages

Shanghai, 11th (Electrocution News Agency) - Acting Minister Chongguang met with a group of reporters today and gave a speech saying that negotiations regarding the Changsha incident were still in progress because the investigation of the actual situation had not yet been completed. The Japanese government hoped for a speedy resolution because there was a precedent of the Nanjing and Hankou incidents. The preliminary investigation by Japanese Consul Kasuya in Changsha was scheduled to be completed on the 9th, but the official report had not yet been received. The investigator specially dispatched by Foreign Minister Wang should arrive in Changsha by today and begin the investigation. Negotiations on the specifics would begin after both sides had completed their investigations. The investigation would be conducted by either the investigative organs of both parties or a newly formed Sino-Japanese joint investigation commission. However, it had not yet been determined. Naturally, the Japanese side would demand compensation for damages based on the Japanese side's investigation. The National Government had already taken full measures in places such as Hankou and Jiujiang and would certainly not allow a second Changsha incident to reoccur.

Incidents Involving Merchant Ships

Yichang Boiler Explosion

Yesterday, Hakka people at this port from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River received a telegram from Yichang stating that during its voyage upstream from Chongqing, the Yichang, a steamer of the American company, Yangtze Rapid Steamship Company (捷江公司), the boiler in the engine room suddenly exploded due to excessive heat. It is said that the machinery was completely damaged and the hull of the ship was also damaged by the explosion. Whether the crew members were injured is not yet known in detail. This telegram was received by the Hakka community, and the company has not yet provided any detailed information.

Jiang Yu Repairs Bow

The bow of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiang Yu steamer was damaged when it was hit by Jardine Matheson's De He steamer near Huangzhou earlier this month. Yesterday, the Jiang Yu returned to Shanghai and docked at the Yangjiadu wharf at 4:00 PM. The damaged area was above the waterline, and even the anchor hawse was damaged. It was scheduled to dispatch engineers to inspect it this morning and then enter the dock for major repairs. Jardine Matheson has already acknowledged liability for the repair costs.

Collision Between Japanese and German Ships

Nippon Yusen's Rokkakumaru, arriving in Shanghai from Japan, entered the Wusongkou at 9:00 AM on Saturday. It collided with the North German Company's steamer Atoran, which was being operated by Melchers & Co. and was departing at the time because they were unable to avoid each other. The German ship damaged the starboard side of the Rokkakumaru, with the damage extending 20 feet. Fortunately, it was above the waterline, so it was still able to sail and has now gone to Japan for inspection before being repaired.
