Important News

Ministry of Education's Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission Reports on the Organizational Outlines of the Mongolian-Tibetan Schools in Nanjing and Kangding

Regarding the issue of developing Mongolian-Tibetan education, a resolution was passed at the Third Plenary Session and the Second National Education Conference to promote concrete plans for Mongolian-Tibetan education. Based on this resolution, the Ministry of Education decided to establish Mongolian-Tibetan schools in Nanjing and Kangding to quickly train talents urgently needed for the development of Mongolia and Tibet and to provide teachers for local education. The Ministry of Education previously drafted organizational outlines for the two schools and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval and requested the allocation of funds to prepare for the establishment. At the 73rd Executive Conference, it was decided to submit the outlines to the Ministry of Education's Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission for further review and response. The Ministry of Education's Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission repeatedly consulted and coordinated, and the organizational outlines for the two schools were revised in detail. Yesterday, the Commission responded to the Executive Yuan for approval. The organizational outlines for the two schools are recorded as follows:

Organizational Outline of the National Nanjing Mongolian-Tibetan School

1. This school is named the National Nanjing Mongolian-Tibetan School.

2. This school is established to prepare Mongolian-Tibetan students for higher education and to train Mongolian-Tibetan talents urgently needed in various fields.

3. This school is directly under the Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission and is supervised and guided by the Ministry of Education.

4. This school has the following classes: A. Special Training Class: According to the current practical needs of Mongolia and Tibet, the law, politics, economics, and education classes will be opened first, and then classes in agriculture, forestry, animal husbandry, industry, and commerce will be added successively. The duration of study is set at two years. B. Middle School Class: Adopt a 3-3 system, with both junior and senior levels and a high school department. The high school department can be divided into general and normal subjects. C. Political Training Personnel Training Class: Established to train current Mongolian-Tibetan civil servants. The duration of study is limited to six months. E. Remedial Class: Established for Mongolian-Tibetan students who cannot attend the special training class or middle school class. First, open one or two classes. D. Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Research Class: Established for those who specialize in researching Mongolian-Tibetan affairs. First, open one class with a duration of study of at least two years. After graduation, they will be sent to work in Mongolian-Tibetan areas.

5. The admission qualifications for each class in this school are as follows: A. Special Training Class: Graduates of senior high school or those with equivalent qualifications are eligible. B. Senior High School: Graduates of junior high school or those with equivalent qualifications are eligible. Junior High School: Graduates of elementary school or those with equivalent qualifications are eligible. C. Political Training Personnel Training Class: Current civil servants in Mongolia and Tibet are eligible. D. Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Research Class: Graduates of schools above senior high school are eligible (not limited to Mongolian-Tibetan students). E. Remedial Class: Those with qualifications equivalent to those in clauses A or B are eligible.

6. The number of students in the special training class and middle school class is based on the number stipulated by the Ministry of Education. The number of students in the remedial class, political training personnel training class, and Mongolian-Tibetan affairs research class is limited to between 60 and 80.

7. The school will provide students with meals, accommodation, textbooks, uniforms, and other expenses.

8. For the sake of practical training for students in the high school normal class or normal quick training class, this school may designate or specially contract nearby elementary schools as practical training institutions.

9. This school will have one principal, who will be appointed or assigned by the Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

10. The teachers of this school are divided into full-time and part-time, and they will be hired by the principal.

11. This school will have one director of academic affairs, one director of administrative affairs, and one director of student affairs. There will be three to five student affairs officers and one school doctor. All will be hired by the principal. There will be one document clerk, one accountant, and one general affairs officer. There will be four to eight administrative staff and six to ten clerks. All will be appointed by the principal.

12. This organizational outline will be implemented after being approved by the Executive Yuan. (To be continued)

Ministry of Education Demarcates Various Project Funds for Higher Education

Total Fund of Six Million Yuan

Average Annual Allocation of 300,000 Yuan

The Ministry of Education has already demarcated various funds for higher education projects, excluding universities, colleges, and vocational schools: (1) A fund of two million yuan for academic research awards and subsidies; (2) A fund of one million yuan for special awards for technological inventions and discoveries; (3) A basic fund of two million yuan for printing subsidies; (4) A fund of one million yuan for academic organization subsidies. The above funds total six million yuan and will be allocated over 20 years, with an average annual allocation of 300,000 yuan. Only the interest will be used thereafter.

Ministry of Education Explains Qualifications for the Old System of Middle School

The Ministry of Education previously received a petition from Zhang Yuanding and other graduates of the old system of middle school regarding the equivalence of qualifications between graduates of the old system of middle school and the new system of middle school, and whether they can receive the same treatment as graduates of the old system of normal school when applying to universities. The Ministry of Education issued the following reply: It is known that the qualifications of graduates of the old system of middle school are equivalent to those who have completed one year of study in senior high school. Those who wish to continue their education must pass an entrance examination and be inserted into the second year of senior high school. Regarding the claim in the petition that graduates of the old system of normal school who have served for more than two years are allowed to study at the College of Education of a university, the Ministry has no such explicit order. Let it be known.

Local News

Notice to Tutors of Private Schools

The Municipal Education Bureau will Conduct Periodic Assessments

Those Who Pass Will be Allowed to Establish Schools

Those Who Fail Will be Closed Immediately

In order to rectify private schools, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has decided to hold periodic assessments of private school tutors. The assessment methods were published in a previous report. Yesterday, the Municipal Education Bureau issued Notice No. 66, stating: "It has been found that although private schools in this city have been banned, they still exist. In order to take into account the students' studies and the tutors' livelihoods, we have decided to conduct periodic assessments of tutors. Those who pass the assessment will be allowed to establish improved private schools. Those who fail the assessment must immediately close their private schools. The assessment methods are listed below. All tutors who establish private schools in this city must register on time and wait for the assessment. Do not make a mistake. This is of utmost importance."

Record of the Shanghai County Education Bureau's Bureau Affairs Meeting

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 161st Memorial Week and Bureau Affairs Meeting yesterday morning. Those present were Director Shi, Zheng Guozhai, Sun Tingfang, Lin Weiwen, Yu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Yan Zhongguang, Xi Simu, Cai Xingsan, Yao Xingye, and Wu Renda, Pan Xingsan. Director Shi presided over the meeting, and Pan Xingsan recorded the minutes. After performing the rituals, the report was briefly presented. Matters for discussion included: (1) How to plan and proceed with the establishment of mass schools attached to various county-level agencies as ordered. It was resolved that the department would formulate specific measures and submit them to the next meeting for discussion. (2) Yu Tang People's Education Center reported its establishment and requested registration. It was resolved to send a letter requesting two copies of the attachments to be submitted for filing with the county office. (3) The procedure for changing school districts this year. It was resolved to notify all education commissioners, district offices, and all educational institutions in the county to check and submit school district maps to the county office for filing. (4) Should the principals of the distributed schools in the central district of Tangwan Elementary School be renamed directors from this year onwards? It was resolved to continue using the title of principal. (5) The second district chief requested acceptance of the Tangmin Elementary School building project. It was resolved to reply to the district to inform the original person in charge to submit the school building drawings, construction details, and final accounts for the county to send personnel to inspect and accept. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

The Success of the Chinese Language Textbook for Senior High School from the World Bookstore

The textbooks for junior and senior high school published by the World Bookstore have become popular throughout the country for a time, and the education community has unanimously praised them. In particular, the Chinese language textbook for senior high school from the Bureau is recognized by the world as an unprecedented creation. The reason is that Chinese language teaching has become the most important issue in recent years. One reason is the lack of good textbooks, and the second is the lack of effective teaching methods. The two are mutually causal. Now, the Chinese language textbook for senior high school from the World Bookstore completely applies scientific methods to edit and identify literary styles, study the relationship between literature and the times, and literary principles as the three major focuses of Chinese language research. It is compiled into a very organized textbook, consisting of three volumes divided into six books. The first volume, upper and lower, is for the study of literary styles; the second volume, upper and lower, is for literary history; and the third volume, upper and lower, is for literary theory. The three volumes are consistently connected but can also be independent of each other. As for the level, it is gradual, and the goal is from near to far. The annotations are simple and appropriate, and both literary words and thoughts are emphasized. They are all carefully considered, which has opened up a new path for Chinese language teaching. Now, dozens or hundreds of schools in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Guangzhou, Xiamen, and other places have scheduled to adopt the book as a textbook. It is heard that in addition to using high-quality wood-free paper for printing, the Bureau is now planning to print another edition on Swedish paper with even lower prices to provide for self-study and seek popularization.

Wang Buxian's Bestselling English Conversation and Letter Writing Model

The two books, "English Conversation Model" and "English Letter Writing Model," written by English writing expert Mr. Wang Buxian and published by the Commercial Press, have been adopted by many middle schools in various provinces and cities. The "Conversation Model" is divided into 41 chapters, listing all the sentences needed inside and outside the school, in commercial communication, meetings, speeches, discussions, and daily life. They are printed side by side with extremely fluent vernacular translations, making it easier for scholars to understand. It is truly the newest and most unique conversation reader. The "Letter Writing Model" has 25 chapters, detailing the methods and regulations for writing various letters in social, commercial, and administrative settings. In addition to listing sample articles, it also provides a variety of information for scholars to use. The Chinese annotations at the end of each chapter are particularly complete.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

Daughter: Mom, please put more vinegar in this fried noodles, I like the sour taste the most.

Mother: Child, vinegar hinders development. You can't eat too much, or you won't grow up and will always be like a child.

Daughter: Then I can ride the tram for free for the rest of my life and save on clothing material when making clothes. Isn't that good?

Husband: I plan to dismiss the cook and have you cook the meals.

Wife: Didn't you previously complain that I didn't cook well?

Husband: But a good cook cooks too well.

Wife: What do you mean by that?

Husband: The doctor said I've been eating too much and have already planted the seeds of a stomach disease. If you cook, I can eat less.

Pastor: Mr. Wang, why haven't you been coming to my church lately?

Mr. Wang: Because your church causes me unpleasant feelings in three ways. First, I get sleepy listening to your sermons. Second, the sound of the hymns annoys me. Third, I first met my wife while attending church in your church, and later we also got married there.

Jiong Yuan Random Notes

— Tianxu Wosheng

Liu Wende, an old man from Jilin, grew two horns on his head. The Japanese hired him at an annual salary of ten thousand gold to go to Japan for biological research. I think, perhaps his father or grandfather, or even himself, was a specialist in producing and selling deer antlers. They raised a deer, hoping every day for its antlers to grow, diligently seeking profit. His mother or wife served as a provider of fodder, treating the deer like a deity. As a result, thoughts solidified into form, leading to this outcome. I have seen a friend who studied Buddhism. After more than ten years, his earlobes drooped like Buddhist beads. After more than thirty years, a round mark appeared on his forehead and between his eyebrows, like the image of the Buddha in paintings. However, my friend Wang Ernan, who does not need to be an old man, is seventy-nine years old this year, and his ears and forehead are already like the above. As for the Buddha-image, only his two ears are so far. As for what is recorded in past records that transformations into objects are mostly near delusional. Therefore, the Ma Yi school often says that appearances follow the mind; this is indeed because they have seen many people. In the past, there was a friend named Guan Hanqing who admired Guan Yu's character since childhood, so his eyebrows and eyes were like the portrait, except without a beard. Wang Er Ma, a performer in Shanghai, who is used to playing Guan Gong, looks absolutely like him on stage. And Xia Yuerun also plays Guan Gong often, so he has some resemblance. As for Mei Lanfang, Cheng Yanqiu, Xun Huisheng, and Shang Xiaoyun, who specialize in cross-dressing, their words and actions become feminine, which is enough to support the saying that appearances follow the mind. I suspect Liu Wende being a deer antler merchant is just an ideal, but it can also be tested on ordinary people to see if it is possible. For example, extend your right arm, stare at a small raised piece of flesh on the arm, and think with all your heart that this flesh can bulge up like a ball. Then, focus your mind, concentrate your attention, and stare without blinking. This flesh will gradually rise and become higher. All kinds of diseases are created by the mind, and a mind like Yao or Jie will appear on the face, which is exactly the same principle.

Detailed Records of the Hua Dong University Summer Conference (Part 2)

— Xiao Meng

Vegetarianism: Putuo is a sea island managed by monks. All the residents of the island are vegetarian. Even canned meat dishes are not available. Generally, those who love meat have a state of mind of not eating without meat. The Youth Association officials shipped canned food from Shanghai to Putuo, but they were exhausted in a few days. After the canned food was gone, the amount of food also decreased greatly. Some admired the beautiful scenery of Putuo and wanted to become monks, but at this point, they dispelled this idea. When returning to Shanghai, they were like hungry people who didn't pick their food. The Ningbo dishes prepared in the ship's steerage were all scrambled for a taste.

Sightseeing: The people in the conference always take an afternoon tour every day, divided into teams. The organized teams often take schools as units. Someone from a certain school came to the conference with only one person, which was very boring. It is necessary to temporarily break the closed-door policy. When the group was touring, they saw watermelons and picked them to eat. Some exchanged a silver dollar for six watermelons and four cantaloupes. They were sweet and fresh, and the skin could be removed with fingers. It was really rare. A certain student was walking halfway and saw a statue of Buddha, so he sat next to it and put his hat on the Buddha's head to take a picture together. The monks were not angry at first and stood by and laughed. Later, when they saw four or five pilgrims passing by without throwing a penny, they became angry, so the student said, "Sir, please understand yourself, we rely on him for food." The teams mostly rode bicycles for sightseeing. The sedan carriers in the temple put the title of "extremely rude" on the members, but because of the large number of people, they were not afraid of them.

Lawyer: Among the members, there is a famous lawyer from Shanghai, Mr. So-and-so, whose eloquent speeches are quite admired by his colleagues. In his free time, he often gathers a dozen people to discuss "criminals" and "laws" as a pleasure. The number of people freely joining this group increased day by day. The closest to him were the students from Shanghai University. This lawyer has been away from school life for many years and is busy in society all day long. He can actually split himself up and join this group as a student. It is really a strange thing. At first, some wanted to ask him various questions, but they were afraid that he would ask for consultation fees after returning to Shanghai, so they hesitated. It was not until a few days later that they realized it was all overthinking.

Farewell: On the last day of the conference, the members exchanged addresses and took many group photos. Some wanted to extend the conference period. When parting, the sound of "See you again someday" was endless, just like "Hope to see you again."

This conference leaders have sacrificed a lot of time and money. General students have benefited from physical, mental, intellectual and social benefit, which is the efforts of the summer conference preparatory committee.

Xiao Chang Xin News

— Qiu Xu

The mountains and peaks of Changshan Yushan area of ​​Zhejiang are high and rugged, and the ports and forks are vertical and horizontal. It takes about half a month by boat from Changshan to Hangzhou, so travelers feel quite inconvenient. The railway authorities have seen this and discussed the construction of a branch road named Xiao Chang (Xiaoshan to Changshan) light railway. The journey is about 700 miles long, and the rails are laid along the foothills to avoid occupying farmland. However, the whole road project is quite large, so it is planned to build the Xiao Zhu (Xiaoshan to Zhuji) section first. It is heard that this section is now under active construction and is expected to be completed by next spring and open to traffic first. It is said that the locomotives needed are the ones currently running on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line. New locomotives have also been ordered from Germany for the Shanghai-Hangzhou line. Once the new locomotives arrive, they can be installed separately. It is also heard that Minister Sun of the Ministry of Railways personally visited the engineering office of the section last month to inspect everything and was very satisfied. In the future, when the entire road is completed and opened to traffic, Hangzhou and Changshan can be reached in one day, which is much more convenient than traveling by boat.

Recording Zhang Huichong's Magic

— Shen Ying

Movie star Zhang Huichong has long been studying magic. Five or six years ago, he showed his skills at the Carlton Theater. This spring, he was again invited by the Central Grand Theater to perform magic on stage for half an hour along with the Yellow Sea Pirate film he starred in. His quick and magical transformations were praised by those who saw him. Recently, the foreign magician Nie Geladi came to Shanghai, calling himself the King of Magic and saying that his large repertoire could not be performed by other magicians. Zhang Jun thought that his words were too arrogant and despised Chinese people. Therefore, last month, he publicly performed the magic that Nie claimed that others could not perform for the Chinese people at the Central Grand Theater. Such as Nie's performance of "Crushing Women", "Waist Chop Beauty" and Silk Scarf Illusion and other programs are extremely wonderful and won the welcome of the audience. Zhang Jun's trial performance was successful. Now, starting from August 14th, he has been invited by the Xia Ling Peck Theater to perform formally for Chinese and foreign audiences. It is heard that his performance programs include the "Water Escape" and "Thousand Stone" programs that Zhang Jun recently invented, in addition to melting and performing the magic of Nie Gelakade and other schools.

Supplement to Anecdotes of Mr. Sheng Xingchuan

— Qing Song Jushi

Unchanged Scholarly Style: The folk customs of Ningdu, Jiangxi Province are fierce and the scholar spirit is rampant. There are Zhao and Wu two Mingjings who are cunning and good at writing. They wear tiger hats and combine with officials to arbitrarily make decisions in the countryside, and the roads are viewed with caution. There is a woman named Quan, whose surname is Liang and married Hong Junsheng in the same village. The lady is newly widowed and naturally beautiful. Zhao and Wu have coveted it for a long time. One day, they saw that the parents-in-law were out, so they broke in and violated it. The woman suffered this humiliation and wanted to die. The father-in-law knew the truth and complained to the magistrate. The magistrate was greedy and confused. Zhao and Wu offered a thousand gold to frame the woman for having a mulberry tryst and accused the father-in-law of suing and placed him in prison, while the two were free from the law. At that time, Mr. Sheng Xingchuan visited Ningdu, and heard about the incident and secretly visited to find out the truth. He summoned the magistrate and rebuked him, saying, "You covet gold and ruin your integrity. How can this be human? I am a Fengxian official and have the duty to maintain customs and redress grievances. Bind Zhao and Wu for me." The magistrate complied and bound them. Mr. Sheng slapped the table and shouted, "You rely on the magic power of money to forcibly violate the chaste woman of a family, coerce the magistrate to reverse the truth and turn it into a wrong. This court has long known that you are colluding with each other and doing all kinds of evil. You are truly beasts in clothing. What do you have to say?" The two knew it was difficult to escape punishment, and they confessed the truth to the court, released the father-in-law from prison, and put the two to justice and impeached the Ningdu magistrate from office. At that time, those who heard it were happy and praised Sheng Qingtian, and the scholarly style of Ningdu was respected.

Caring for the Poor After Relief: There was a man named Liu, who was a fellow villager of Mr. Sheng and had a close relationship. When Mr. Sheng passed the imperial examination, Liu was assigned to the Luojiang County of Sichuan Province. As a scholar, he was not good at flattering the magistrate and remained honest and upright throughout his life. After his death, he was poor and owed a thousand gold to the government. The superiors urged him to pay it back as soon as possible, and the coffin was stopped in the wilderness, and there was no way to return to his hometown. His wife and children cried sadly. Mr. Sheng was presiding over the examination in Sichuan and felt unbearable pain for the coldness of human relations. He asked the superiors to voluntarily compensate and persuaded scholars and people to help him. At that time, three hundred gold were collected from the wheat boat. Liu's family was able to transport the coffin back. Mr. Sheng gave another two hundred gold to manage his family. Both the living and the dead felt the Yin virtue. It is not luck that he reached the age of ancient times and reached old age. It is appropriate.

New Knowledge of the Family

— Edited by Tianxu Wosheng

Homemade fruit dew wine or ice jelly or cool rice cakes and fruit soup. Using Invincible brand fruit dew, it is all beautiful and extraordinary. Using almond dew to make almond cheese is even more beautiful. Adding almond dew to milk or soy milk can resolve phlegm, relieve coughs, heal the lungs, and moisten the intestines. The effect is very obvious. Drinking this in autumn is more effective than medicine for preventing coughs and dysentery. Lemon dew is suitable for summer. It clears away heat, relieves heat, can cure stomach pain, and prevents epidemics, cholera, and prickly heat. It is much safer than cold food sold in the market. If you want to be cool, mix it with ice water. The taste is the same as Dutch water. It is a pity that the glass bottle is too big and the postage is inconvenient, which makes people far away sigh. (Fang Chengde)

Xu's Note: The fruit dew can be concentrated to ten times or even a hundred times, but the amount used is not appropriate, so it is often unsatisfactory. Therefore, it is not produced and sold. If you want to use this as a business item in a distant port, please contact us by letter, and we will have a way. The approximate cost is 500 yuan, and you can get about 25% profit, and you can also produce and sell white rose wine, which is made with local shochu and fragrance. The price of each jin of fragrance is only 1.2 cents. If you want to try it out, just send 5 yuan in postage stamps to the agency, and we will send you various types and their preparation methods for trial production.

There are many ways to make ice cream. Some contain too much water, which leads to the formation of ice flowers that are sandy. Some contain too much powder, which is as hard as a cake and unpleasant. Some contain too much milk and soften like cream. All of these are shortcomings. The best ice cream in Shanghai was formerly made by Huitong on Nanjing Road. It was fat and beautiful like butter from the borderlands. It is a pity that the cost was too high, so the price was high and the diners gradually thinned out. I made it myself in its style. The finished product is excellent. Twelve eggs a month. First, beat the egg whites into a froth. Then, beat the egg yolks in another container, add three pounds of fresh milk and one pound of fruit dew and mix them thoroughly. Then, gradually add one pound of six-grain flour and mix it into a slurry to ensure that there are no particles. If there are particles, they should be fished out, dissolved in cold water, and mixed in again. Then, combine it with the egg white froth and put it in a shaking bucket. Surround the bucket with crushed ice and add salt. For every ten pounds of ice, two pounds of salt should be added so that the ice melts easily and gets very cold. Shake for only thirty minutes and it is done. Do not open the lid temporarily. Cover the top of the bucket with a damp cloth so that it can be stored for a long time. The product thus produced is enough for twelve people to eat and have plenty left over. The cost is only 1.5 yuan. The banana dew of the Invincible brand is the best for the fruit dew used. Each dozen pounds only costs 2.4 yuan, which is much cheaper and more beautiful than using fruit juice and sugar. If you want it to form sand and ice chips, add two pounds of cold water when mixing, so that it contains more water. (Ri Zhi)

Dance Knowledge (Part 2)

— Bu Wu Zhi He

(1) If a female guest does not want to dance for any reason, she must have a reasonable excuse, such as being unwell or feeling tired, and must express deep apologies. However, after this statement, she must not dance with other male guests. (1) Tea dance should be waited until after tea snacks are served, and meal dance should be waited until after soup and fish are served. (1) When leading a female guest for the first time, you must see how good at dancing she is. If she is very good at dancing, you can gently touch her shoulder and use your arm movements to guide her. In this way, the chest can be separated and the demeanor is elegant. However, if you encounter a clumsy dancer, it is still better to hug her tightly to avoid tripping and bumping toes due to being too polite, leading to falling and losing your composure. (1) When dancing in hot weather, pay attention to sweaty hands getting the female guest's clothes dirty (especially those wearing evening dresses). It is best to lightly touch the back of the index finger and wrist of the dance partner, and loosen your hands from time to time to avoid raising the clothes. Be sure to avoid holding the whole palm tightly. It is best to wear gloves. (1) In hot weather, you must pay attention to your appearance. If you are sweating, your veins are bulging, your face is red, and you are panting, you should rest, tidy up your appearance, and wipe away sweat. You should not be rude or use paper to fan yourself, etc. (1) When the music stops, you should stop lightly and pat her hand, listen to the music and continue playing, and then dance again. If the dance partner shows signs of fatigue at the end of the first song, you should stop. However, you cannot stop dancing before the music stops, otherwise it will inevitably attract attention. (1) When dancing with a female guest who is not very familiar, you should not dance a too lively step that is difficult for the other party to cope with and feel sorry for themselves, thus making them unhappy. (1) You should not refuse to dance if you have been requested by a female guest to dance. If there are special reasons, you must also set up a word of tactful refusal. (1) You should always check yourself in terms of manners, and apologize if you feel that you have been negligent. (1) If you are not familiar with slightly complicated dances such as Polonaise or Tango, you should refrain from dancing when the music starts, or if you can dance but dance with a female guest who is not familiar with this kind of dance, it is easy to cause improper etiquette, so you must pay attention. (1) It is easy to attract attention when there are occasional inappropriate things in social situations, but you must deal with them calmly and calmly to quell the public's ridicule. Do not be cramped and ashamed, which will only lead to publicity and become uncontrollable. (1) No matter what kind of dance posture, it should be beautiful. For example, when dancing Foxtrot, it should be lively and brisk, Polonaise should be natural and lazy, Waltz should be beautiful and gentle, Tango should be charming and gentle. Avoid hunching back, snake waist, crooked head, bent hands, shaking shoulders, restraining legs and other ugly attitudes. When dancing, words must be respectful and polite. Avoid being humble and rude. (1) When attending a dance party, you must not be full of sorrow and make the whole seat unhappy. You should try to make a happy face and cheer up. Otherwise, you can refuse to come so that others will not be unhappy because of you. (Appendix) At tea parties, female guests are mostly responsible for serving tea, adding sugar, pouring milk, and serving snacks. Men are responsible for serving tea, coffee, or fruit juice after meals. If alcohol is served, sweet wine is appropriate. If the dance partner is beautiful, serving mint wine, peach cheeks and willow eyebrows will reflect each other, and the red lights and green wine are enough to intoxicate without drinking. If men want to drink, they can only drink beer or stronger alcoholic drinks to show the outline of their beard. If you don't want to drink, you can order ginger beer or ginger ale. Otherwise, ordering a cup of milk is equal to being in a nursery.

Warmth in the Heart (2) (5) (2)

— Bao Tianxiao

Episode 13: Who Plants Fortune and Unintentionally Obtains a Diamond Ring? Only This Karma Sings a Gold Thread

At that moment, Zuo Shichen suddenly encountered a frustrating and frustrating thing. What do you say it is? It turned out that his beloved son died. This child of his was three years old according to the Chinese way of calculating age. According to the foreign way of calculating, it was less than three years old, only twenty-six months old. He was already learning to speak. This child had a smart face, but he unexpectedly contracted a sudden infantile convulsion, and the onset was at twelve o'clock at night. He was caught off guard. However, Zuo Shichen believed in Western medicine. Near where he lived was a hospital opened by a Western church, and there was a female doctor who was famous for specializing in pediatrics. The quickest way was to immediately knock on the door of that hospital and ask that female doctor to come for a consultation. At that time, there was only a maid and a carriage driver in Zuo Shichen's house. Because he thought it would be difficult for the carriage driver to explain clearly, he decided to go himself. He simply left the carriage driver at home and hired a streetcar to come to the hospital and knocked on the door for a long time. The gatekeeper of the hospital finally asked with a sleepy and hazy tone, "Who is it?" Zuo Shichen said, "Please see the doctor, thank you for opening the door." The gatekeeper said with lingering anger, "Please see the doctor? What doctor do you want to see in the middle of the night? Can't you ask a doctor to come during the day tomorrow?" Zuo Shichen felt a little angry in his heart when he heard his words. He thought that the arrival of disease is not like many regular people. It does not patronize people at night. Disease is an evil demon that does not know the time. It comes whenever it wants to. The duty of a doctor is to defeat the evil demon of disease. When encountering an emergency, the doctor should set off at any time, regardless of night or day. Treating an emergency is like putting out a fire. How can you slowly wait until tomorrow? Moreover, the family's hope for a doctor is like a living Bodhisattva saving lives. When Zuo Shichen went out, his wife was holding the sick child in her arms, her eyes filled with tears. She repeatedly said, "Can you ask that doctor to come right away? Promise him whatever medical expenses he wants." It was as if the doctor's hand touched the child's head and the illness would disappear immediately. It was just that he encountered such a gatekeeper when he knocked on the hospital door. Zuo Shichen thought that the child was probably difficult to save. The first hurdle was unlucky. But he still begged him to open the door. He thought that the gatekeeper only knew the gatekeeper's duties, and it would be useless to say anything to him. If he agreed to open the door, he could talk to the hospital official, or if he was lucky, he could talk to the doctor directly. How could he know that the doctor would not be willing to come when he saw my urgent request?

Financial and Gold Markets Continue to Decline

Trend is Unpredictable, Resulting in a Downward Trend

The Silver Dollar Market Was Slightly Better at the Beginning of the Week

Market Overview

The business situation in the financial sector is inherently dull during the late summer and early autumn. Therefore, the daily situation is unusually quiet. The buying and selling of foreign funds and the slow digestion of goods, as well as the supply and demand of silver funds, are not significant. As a result, the amount of collections and settlements is becoming increasingly scarce, and even interbank lending transactions have been interrupted. However, yesterday was Monday, and the market atmosphere was slightly better than usual. Bank collections and settlements were also quite prosperous, but the digestion of foreign funds remained sluggish.

Interest Rate for Short-Term Loans

(Foreign Interest Rate) The morning market was at 7 qian, 2 fen, 9 li, 1 hao and 2 hu and a half. The noon market was at 7 qian, 2 fen, 9 li, 3 hao and 7 hu and a half. The result seemed to be 3 hao and 7 hu and a half higher than the market price of the previous day. However, due to the small amount of sales, there was ultimately no possibility of rising. It may also be that it is hovering and unable to make any significant changes. (Silver Interest Rate) The loose and excessive silver supply has reached its extreme in recent days. Every day, it is either 2 fen or a free loan. Although the morning market silver interest rate opened at 2 fen yesterday, the noon market was still a free loan. There was no market for negotiated rates, let alone silver listings.

Subsidiary Coin Market Situation

Jiangnan small silver dollars remained firm. The morning market was at 6 qian, 4 fen and 3 li. The noon market was at 6 qian, 4 fen and 2 li. The result was comparable to the noon market of the previous day. The transaction volume was 4,000 jiao in the morning market and 2,000 jiao in the noon market. The Guangdong small silver dollars were at 6 qian, 1 fen, 5 li and 7 hao and a half in the morning market and 6 qian, 1 fen, 6 li and 7 hao and a half in the noon market. The fluctuations between the two markets were 1 li, and it was 1 li and 2 hao and a half higher than the morning market of the previous day. The transaction volume was 85,000 jiao in the morning market and 90,000 jiao in the noon market. Copper coins remained at 391,000 wen.

Silver Dollar Inflow and Outflow

(Silver Funds) Yesterday, there were no new records of bank collections and settlements, only routine collections and settlements. Chinese banks collected and settled over 300,000 yuan of drafts, foreign banks collected and settled over 2.3 to 2.4 million yuan of drafts, special drafts were over 1.3 million yuan, advances were 1 million yuan, and various freight, tax and miscellaneous collections and settlements were over 1.1 million yuan. Out of storage was 1.3 million yuan. Japanese banks collected and settled 4.6 to 4.7 million yuan of various funds, with 700,000 yuan going out of storage. Money shops and silver firms collected and settled over 39 million yuan of single drafts, negotiated drafts were over 3.9 million yuan, remittance drafts from various routes were over 1.1 million yuan, and cash collected was over 2 million yuan, all to be deposited in storage. (Foreign Funds) The morning market saw 1.19 million yuan in remittance drafts, and the noon market saw 778,000 yuan. Banknotes in the noon market were 10,000. Over-the-counter banknotes in the morning market were 165,000, and in the noon market were 90,000. Bank transactions were 500,000 in the morning market and 450,000 in the noon market. Collections and settlements between foreign bank accounts were over 1.7 million yuan. Banknotes recovered and issued were over 2.1 million yuan. Money shops and foreign firms collected and settled over 5.6 to 5.7 million yuan of single drafts, foreign negotiated drafts were over 1.4 million yuan, foreign short-term loans were over 900,000 yuan, small money shops exchanged banknotes and sold remittance drafts for 700,000 to 800,000 yuan in cash, and over 200,000 yuan of banknotes and cash arrived from various ports, but the amount going out was still only over 300,000 yuan.

Records of the Desolate Financial Scene

The financial industry in Shanghai is currently slightly calm. It is generally expected that it will be prosperous in the autumn. However, trade with other ports is becoming increasingly sluggish. Since the major stimulus in the Guangzhou market, it has inevitably declined. The Hubei businesses have also been affected in the same way, and they have generally reduced lending, even refusing to do much. If cash needs to be shipped, the cash must be remitted by telegraphic transfer before it can be shipped. Otherwise, it may take many days of waiting. It is also heard that the Jiangxi businesses have also been affected by the military situation, and the transportation of goods and remittances has been temporarily suspended. This autumn, various goods will not be handled as usual. In addition, land transportation in the northern routes is blocked, and goods are stagnant. The provinces of Henan and Hunan are even more desolate after the disasters, and it will take time for post-disaster recovery. However, trade with overseas Chinese is still smooth, which is surprising.

The total spot market transaction volume was 15,000 yuan, of which whole sixes accounted for 13,000 yuan, and the rest were extremely scarce. The futures market opened at over 5.7 million yuan in the morning and only over 2.3 million yuan in the afternoon, for a total of over 8 million yuan. Whole sixes and post-disaster relief bonds each accounted for only 400,000 to 500,000 yuan.

Cotton Market in a Slack Situation

The cotton market is flat and weak, and the overall situation is mediocre. Due to the sharp fall and slight rise in US cotton and the recent good weather, the production of new cotton in Hankou and Tongzhou is smooth. Therefore, some Hubei businesses are selling short. Buyers see the environment as unfavorable and dare not raise prices sharply. However, the Ningbo businesses are still increasing their positions. Manufacturers have a calm attitude because their inventory of old cotton is thick and there is enough for immediate use, so there is no need to purchase. The same is true for Japanese factories. The future of the cotton market is still difficult to be optimistic about and must depend on US cotton for changes.

Flour Market Near Firm, Far Weak

Yesterday, the flour market generally showed a hovering trend. Initially, the small report of foreign wheat made people slightly tired. Then, the manufacturers' intention to buy in the near future stimulated the market. However, in the long run, the flour sales could not rise, and the outside buyers had no intention of actively pursuing them. Therefore, the market atmosphere was flat. Judging from this situation, the near term should not be too weak due to the manufacturers' support. If the accumulation of goods in the long term becomes too large, problems will inevitably arise. As a result, the current month was 5 li better than the previous week, September was 2.5 li worse, November-December was 2.5 li worse, and January was 5 li worse.

Near-Term Wheat Deficiencies, Bulls Alone Prosper

Spot Goods, Factory Demand Active...Increased by 5 Fen

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a near-firm and far-flat trend. This was because the short sellers in the current month were actively covering their positions, and there was very little high-quality goods on the market. All the goods did not meet the standards, and they may need to be taken delivery of when the opportunity arises. Therefore, people became nervous and the market turned firm again. In the long term, foreign wheat fell by a small amount of 3 to 4 jiao, and most people were still bearish, so there were few fluctuations. As a result, the current month rose by 4 fen compared to the previous week, September rose by 2 fen, and October to January remained unchanged. Spot wheat had very few high-quality goods arriving, and the source was not abundant. The demand from various factories was still active, so all grades increased by 5 fen. Wheat from Kaisashi, Jiangyan, Qitang, Yaowan, Bengbu, Guandian, Qishu, Xiping, Xinyangzhou, and Hankou, totaling over 7,000 bags, was taken away by factories such as Fuxin and Fufeng.

Silk and Tea Factory Long Silk Exports Slightly Up

Since the summer, long silk exports from silk factories have been quiet for a long time, and the market price has been sluggish. Recently, overseas silk factories have started work, and demand has gradually increased. Yesterday, there was a long silk export message from Marseille, with transactions including 30 bales of superior silk factory long silks from Xinfu, priced at 180 taels, gradually showing firmness.

European and American Stockpiles, Factory Operations

Yesterday, the foreign silk market in Shanghai continued to show a firm rise because European and American firms, aware that there was not much silk in overseas inventory, took the opportunity to stockpile yellow and white factory silk. However, because the price did not rise high, Chinese merchants were not willing to sell. Yesterday, only Lan Lebi and others took in 80 bales of white factory silk in Shanghai, and Dachang and others took in 50 bales of yellow factory silk, with prices all firm.

Roadside Green Tea, European Sales Slightly Smooth

The market price for the best needle tea has risen by 4 to 5 taels. However, the medium and low-grade goods remained unchanged. Social News

Passing of Mr. Xie Jiezi, Staff Member of This Newspaper

Mr. Xie Jiezi, a staff member of this newspaper, passed away due to pneumonia at 10 PM on August 10th. The encoffining ceremony was held at 3 PM yesterday at his residence, No. 1789, East End of North Zhejiang Road, Hai'ning Road. The funeral procession is scheduled for 1 PM today, with temporary interment at the Xijin Guild Hall. Colleagues, upon hearing the news, have flocked to pay their respects and assist with the arrangements. Mr. Xie, a native of Dantu, was the younger brother of the renowned painter Mr. Xie Gongzhan. After graduating from school, he joined this newspaper's editorial department in 1919, serving diligently without regard for the weather, day or night. He also co-founded the Newspaper Reporters' Association with colleagues to foster camaraderie and exchange knowledge, achieving notable success. Possessing a frail constitution, he also held teaching positions at Minli Middle School and other schools, leading to a gradual weakening of his lungs and subsequent hemoptysis. Following the advice of relatives and friends, he spent over a year recuperating at Meiyuan in Wuxi, significantly restoring his health. However, he soon resumed his duties at the newspaper as before. Recently, due to the need for personnel to promote the West Lake Exposition, this newspaper requested Mr. Xie to serve as an editor. He took on all tasks, large and small, despite his physical condition, and his illness worsened as a result. Most recently, he frequently traveled under the scorching sun due to his wife, Ms. Zhang Shimin's illness, which led to a sudden and severe case of pneumonia. Although he received treatment at Baolong Hospital, medicine proved ineffective, ultimately leading to his demise. Mr. Xie was proficient in poetry and classical prose, and he published books such as "Lakeside Lianyin Grass." He passed away at the young age of thirty-three, his talents tragically unfulfilled. Alas.

Shanghai Market

Market News

Baida Record Company on Sichuan Road declares: Our company released a large batch of new records yesterday, including Xu Biyun's "Yutangchun," Xue Qiongying's "Green Pearl" and "Yellow Crane Tower," Li Jirui's "Hongbi Yuan," "Please Song Ling," "Linked Rings," "Luoma Lake," "Dumu Pass," "The Storm at Fengbo Pavilion," Bai Yukun's "Ksitigarbha," Chen Shanfu's "Offering the Map," "Jinma Gate," "Empress Dowager's Dance," "Walking and Teaching the Son," Rong Lijuan's "Beating the Flower Drum," "Diaochan's Linked Rings," "Visiting Mother," "Creation of the World," Cao Family Three Reds' "Yutangchun," "Sweeping Flowers, Three Drunkennesses," "Spinning Cotton," "Offering the Map," "Accepting the Throne," "Wu Zhaoguan," "South Heavenly Gate," Xiao Kuiguan's "Opera Fan's Biography," Piao Yunlu Jushi's "Yu Chang Sword," "Black Basin," Lü Songsheng's "Cosmic Front," Feng Zhaoliang's "Wujiapo," and dozens of Yangzhou tunes. The four Baida branch stores on the Great Road, Lao Baofang on Edward Road, Xin Baofang on Edward Road, and other branches are all selling them.

Yili Soda Company declares: Our company's various sodas have always been known for their low prices and high quality. This year, we are manufacturing them with distilled water, and the raw materials are pure. Repeated chemical tests have proven that they are the cleanest and free of impurities. As a result, the sales volume is quite high, with demand exceeding supply. The brisk sales in various parts of Nanyang are unmatched by other companies.

Huachang Motor Shop, No. 380 West of Zhengjia Wooden Bridge on Edward Road, declares: Our shop will officially open today. The newly built four-story Western-style building is grand in scale and well-arranged. We specialize in various bicycles, motorcycles, and chartered cars. We have a complete selection of various vehicle parts. We will also hold a big sale for four weeks starting from the opening day to thank our customers for their patronage.

Book Review

Rest

— Chunsen

By Wang Shiwei

In such an evil society filled with demons and monsters, how can we not cause young people to feel pain, sorrow, disappointment, and despair? All feudal relics have formed an iron fence, surrounding us, and what is presented before our eyes is nothing but ghosts and darkness. When we have not yet entered society, we are full of hope. However, after entering, the actual environment is only a fraction of what we imagined. Every day we are exposed to nothing but cold, cruel, hypocritical, and deceitful faces and tedious and rigid work. Thus, naturally, the lively, passionate spirit declines, the nerves and thoughts become numb and dull, and the pure soul is shot with the arrow of wounds. After all, it can no longer endure... endure... And on the path of life, it becomes tired and even disgusted.

Of course, the blame lies in the fact that young people cannot persist to the end and are frightened by the vast unknown future and cannot accept the reality of the social environment. It is impossible to escape the struggle and thoroughly transform it. But on the other hand, such a social system only makes pure young people run into walls everywhere. And because the young people's pure and innocent bodies are often unwilling to cater to the muddy current and pollute their own personality, in such a disparate situation, can we give a young person who has just left school life and entered the real society, who is very confident, a good result? Scene after scene of darkness only disgust themselves, and at the same time, how can they not think about what they should do? Can the environment allow it? They cannot struggle, they cannot struggle. What else can they do? Although everyone says that young people are full of upward will, who knows that the more they are like this, the deeper their troubles are. They seek light in their work, yes, but if they work blindly, what kind of blow should we inflict? We can say, "If this hellish society is not destroyed, the pain of mankind will not be relieved for a single day. If a reasonable and beautiful society is not successfully constructed, the happiness of mankind cannot be obtained for a single day." These words are naturally a bit too far away, but they also show the bad situation in which the young people of the era are. Therefore, while we demand that young people fully express their will to improve and advance, we must also create a new and beautiful society so that young people can develop their personality and unconsciously generate encouraging power. Therefore, if we are strict, we can explain a sentence for our young people: this is mostly the influence given by society.

This book "Rest" is a shout that comes from the practical life of society, an exposure of an evil society, unable to overcome all kinds of oppression, indignation, sorrow, disappointment, pain... so that one has to abandon everything and go to that quiet and clear wave to rest. The author shouted like this: "My death is not suicide, I just want to go to that clear, quiet and cold wave to rest, rest my tired spirit, adjust my withered blood, and soothe my scorched soul - when I recover my original strength, I will fight with this demon society again, I will not die." (Page 85) This rest, this symbol of fatigue in life, can it not arouse a sense of resonance and flow with deep tears of sympathy? Let us see, an extreme opponent of suicide, who recognizes himself as "one of the conscious youths, and even more unwilling to solve personal problems with death and easily abandon his mission" (Page 48), actually "remembered that I was still a strong and lively youth a year ago. I don't know why, but today, a year later, I have to throw myself, throw myself into the arms of death" (Page 84). He is so grieved, "My mother's death is of course a deep wound in my life, but it is this bloody and smelly society that sucks my blood and consumes my energy. It made me lose my schooling, made me do unwanted and cumbersome mechanical work, made my blood boil, made me go crazy, made me suffer from incurable diseases, and finally it forced me to die" (Page 85). Oh, whose misfortune is this? Whose gift is this?

This place contains eleven letters. When I finished reading them in one breath, I couldn't help but feel fire stirring in my heart. I was moved by the flame-like emotions. This society actually sacrificed such a young person. No, in fact, more young people were sacrificed in the same way, right?

He is "...repenting that he should not have studied, but should have been an ignorant and unknowing farmer, tilling and eating a few acres of thin land, serving his old mother morning and evening, and enjoying the natural scenery and the pleasures of family life. It is more carefree than studying. It is not only not expensive, but it can also be engaged in production in farming, and the family is not as debt-ridden as it is now." Therefore, the eighteen-year-old youth who had to end his school life and walk on this dark and dirty social road came with ulterior motives. As a post office clerk, although he "felt a subtle pain because this place has shown the shadow of the devil in my eyes and is smiling at me," he also "felt a kind of unprecedented joy because I thought that this was the first day to earn a meal with my own strength" (Page 7). He hoped to study and work part-time. Unexpectedly, in less than half a month, the so-called plan became a pipe dream and he experienced the unspeakable taste. "I have changed from a lively and vigorous youth into a slave to machines. Just in terms of working hours, from 7 am to 10 pm, there is almost no free time. Even eating is not free, and every meal is swallowed raw and hard, filling the stomach. After putting down the bowl and chopsticks, I have to continue this immortal work" (Page 9). He was even ridiculed by his colleagues because he was a newcomer and was treated with evil intentions of glaring and contempt everywhere, but his work was more tedious than any of his colleagues.

Finally, because the machine was used too violently, he vomited a large mouthful of bright red blood and suffered a near-death illness. His youthful energy disappeared. However, he was still fighting and mustered up the courage to attack, "As long as we work hard, we can get the price." Because -

"The mission of us young people is to use our strength to destroy all the dens of iniquity, use our blood to extinguish all the demonic fires, save the endangered motherland, and transform the dirty society. This is our only goal and responsibility" (Page 47). Unfortunately, his beloved mother passed away. The wound this gave him was that "My mother and I really depend on each other for life. She is the comforter in the depths of my spirit, the light of my life, and the sustenance of my soul. Losing such a mother who is truly worthy of being a mother, all my courage, hope, enthusiasm, and ambitions have melted away" (Page 61). Isn't that so?

At the same time, he also tasted the stimulation of "seeing relatives and friends as having no human feelings." His uncle, when he had just suffered the double wounds of losing his mother and a serious illness, immersed in sadness, viciously forced him to pay back the money borrowed when he returned home for his mother's funeral to achieve the purpose of annexing the family's property. And he discovered that his illness had reached a point where it could not be cured. So he shed everything and decided on his plan. He told us,

"I am extremely opposed to self-proclaimed conscious young people committing suicide. Suicide due to a broken heart, although it has its own meaning, is already something that we Chinese youths in this era should avoid and regard as inappropriate. As for suicide due to grief and indignation over the evils of society and the decay of the country, if it is not due to sudden madness and the intellect has not disappeared, then it is simply cowardly and incomplete and should be rejected by us. Because I believe that if we truly want to save the country and truly want to transform society, we should use our energy and blood to do some practical work in exchange for some price - but I am now a person with exhausted energy and withered blood. I really have no energy and no blood, no nothing."

Oh, really, "We are now in the period of youthful thought, unrestrained passion, and the pursuit of truth, beauty, and goodness. Unfortunately, we are born in this era and this society, and what we come into contact with is darkness, filth, and evil everywhere. How can we not wound our pure souls and make us feel grief, indignation, and disappointment?" As for this tragedy, what we want to respect is his cry that has come from the real life of society, although there are inevitably some places where he is self-defeating. But can we not see that his steadfast, persevering, and fearless spirit is revealed everywhere? Oh, our eighteen-year-old young warrior has been taken away by society. Is this our young people's vitality?

I can't help but feel full of emotion. In short, although this book is close to being pessimistic and sentimental, we can discover how much of our society's inside story there is.

Women's Life Submission Guidelines

(1) The text should be about the discussion of women's issues, domestic and foreign news about women, descriptions of women's lives, essays, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) Pictures should be about women's issues.

(3) Photos should be about women's news, women's issues, and women's lives. Individuals and groups are very welcome.

(4) Each text should not exceed 2,000 words.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and do not write the words carelessly. Western writing can be omitted. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please specify that the submission is for the Women's Life Department.

(9) All submissions will not be returned, whether published or not. If you need to return it, you should declare it in advance and attach sufficient postage stamps.

(10) The remuneration is 3 yuan, 2 yuan, and 1 yuan per thousand words. The same applies to pictures and photos. If there are special submissions, the remuneration will be calculated separately.
